  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ecf52e5b-e6f1-4592-943c-eaff9b7d57cb'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer7378619351671557050">Violet Winters once had it all but lost it when her husband was murdered by a criminal madman. During a cold winter night Violet has to leave her warm bed to tell her neighbor to turn the music down. And that’s when she meets sinister, scarred, scarily attractive security specialist, Joe Callahan. <br/><br/>She wants to deny it, but Violet can’t beat back the hunger she feels for Jo</span>
  <span id="freeText7378619351671557050" style="display:none">Violet Winters once had it all but lost it when her husband was murdered by a criminal madman. During a cold winter night Violet has to leave her warm bed to tell her neighbor to turn the music down. And that’s when she meets sinister, scarred, scarily attractive security specialist, Joe Callahan. <br /><br />She wants to deny it, but Violet can’t beat back the hunger she feels for Joe so she gives in again and again. Feeling it himself, Joe feeds Vi’s hunger, breaking his own rules to keep her in his bed. <br /><br />Even though Violet had only one man in her life, she’s sure Joe is giving her the signals and Vi decides she’s ready to take a second chance at life and, maybe, love. But Violet doesn’t know the dark secrets in Joe’s past, secrets so soul-wrenching, they’ve drained him dry. With nothing left to give, Joe’s determined to live his life alone and he breaks Violet’s heart. <br /><br />Crushed by Joe’s betrayal, Violet comes to terms with the fact that, no matter what signals he gave, Joe was not theirs to win. But Violet’s husband’s murderer is obsessed with her and heartbreak again haunts the door of the Winters home. When it does Joe is forced to face the knowledge that he can’t fight Violet’s pull, she’s under his skin and filled him full to bursting. <br /><br />Joe needs to win her back and put his life on the line to keep Violet safe. But, having had it all once, can Violet endure losing Joe?</span>
  <a data-text-id="7378619351671557050" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

I&#39;m not really into reading books with love-triangle, they aren&#39;t really my thing. I didn&#39;t notice that some people have tagged it as one before I started reading it! Just got to the part where the alternative love interest has made an entrance.</a>

The reason the author uses the triangle theme (for a small portion of the book) is more as a stepping stool to the VERY OBVIO<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">It's not very prominent. The reason the author uses the triangle theme (for a small portion of the book) is more as a stepping stool to the VERY OBVIOUS love match. I don't like the triangle theme at all, but because of the reason for the triangle (I don't want to give it away) it did not detract from the book.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_481613625" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/481613625?book_show_action=true">Dec 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2017-audio">2017-audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer481613625" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15085246679241069310"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505610396i/23940860.jpg' width='350' height='140' alt='“description"/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Can Kristen Ashley write a bad book??? I think not. This may be my new favorite of hers. Couldn’t get enough of Joe and Violet! I fell in love with this story. An amazing read! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505610396i/23940861.jpg' width='400' height='550' alt='“description"/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Violet has recently moved to ‘the burg’ with her two teenage daughters from Chicago. Her husband a cop, the man she was with since she was a teenager was murdered over a year ago, so now its just her and her girls. One night, she hears a lot of music coming from her neighbors house in the middle of the night. Sh</span>
  <span id="freeText15085246679241069310" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505610396i/23940860.jpg" width="350" height="140" alt='“description"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Can Kristen Ashley write a bad book??? I think not. This may be my new favorite of hers. Couldn’t get enough of Joe and Violet! I fell in love with this story. An amazing read! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505610396i/23940861.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt='“description"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Violet has recently moved to ‘the burg’ with her two teenage daughters from Chicago. Her husband a cop, the man she was with since she was a teenager was murdered over a year ago, so now its just her and her girls. One night, she hears a lot of music coming from her neighbors house in the middle of the night. She doesn’t want it to wake her girls, so she goes to check it out. Thats when she meets her neighbor, Joe Callahan. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505610396i/23940863.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt='“description"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Joe makes quite an impression on Violet, and not necessarily in a good way. Joe, who goes by ‘Cal’, is in the security business. He travels a lot for work. Joe is a bad ass alpha male. He is tough and rugged on the outside, on the inside he is empty. He has a damaged past. He can be a jerk some of the book, but he is just so damn lovable. <br><br>Joe and Violet’s ‘relationship’ starts out as a ‘booty call’ as Vi calls it. She just can’t resist Joe. He doesn’t want to form a connection with her, he doesn’t do relationships, hasn’t for seventeen years, but there is something about Violet that is different. He knows it right away. Joe knows he is empty. <br><b>
  <blockquote>“Nothing can fill you up,” she stated.<br>“Nope,” he agreed again.<br>“You won’t let it.”<br>“Barrel’s got a hole in the bottom, buddy, everything leaks out no matter how much you pour in.”</blockquote>
</b><br>Violet is given no choice in the matter. Joe pretty much dismisses her, and pretty harshly. You will think Joe is a giant asshole for a good part of the book, but he has his reasons. She tries to move on with the ‘nice cop’, but its hard. Eventually, Joe realizes he made a mistake. A HUGE mistake. He wants her and the girls back and he takes whats his. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You’re mine, the girls are mine. I’m stakin’ my claim with you right now and, you force it, I’ll do it with him too.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>And one of my favorite parts of the book...<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You know that hole?”he asked.<br>“What?” she asked back.<br>“You were right. You and the girls plugged it.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Once Joe and Vi were together... I just loved it. I couldn’t keep the smile off of my face! Those two together, two damaged people finding each other, it just makes my heart happy. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505610396i/23940864.jpg" width="400" height="330" alt='“description"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Things couldn’t be easy for these two, even after going through everything they went through, healing each other, loving each other. There was a ton of drama. The man who murdered Vi’s husband and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Her brother Sam... OMG I cried like a baby at that scene!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> is after Violet. He wants her and he won’t stop until he has her. He is a straight up creeper, but a powerful man from Chicago. He is the reason Vi had to move. You know in ‘the burg’ there is a lot of drama, stalkers, action etc. On a side note- It was great seeing Colt and Feb again too :D<br><br>Not only did I absolutley love Violet and Joe, Violet’s daughters were just so awesome. They were in the book a lot. Just loved them both. Especially Keira. She was a firecracker. Their relationship with their mom was great- <i>Momalicious</i>, and I loved how they interacted with Joe. That was one of my favorite parts of the book. How the girls and Joe were together, how they accepted each other and became a family. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Kiera was a magnet for trouble. Kate would rather die a thousand bloody, painful deaths than break a rule or get into trouble. Keira would make a deal with the devil for a pair of killer shoes and not even blink.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Joe and Violet were HOT together. They were sweet together. Both of thier stories and pasts were heartbreaking, but I loved how they were able to come together, heal one another. It was just beautiful.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505610396i/23940862.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt='“description"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kristen Ashley: I will forever be a fan of yours, woman! I will read anything you write! This one was just great. Such a beautiful and fantastic book about love, friendship, healing and second chances. If you haven’t read this series yet, you are missing out!!! I give it 5 freaking spectacular stars!!! LOVE LOVE LOVE &lt;3</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1637292707" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1637292707" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1637292707?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1637292707" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2179646783553414280">Just shoot me. This fucking book! I wanted to murder the main guy. He is an alpha asshole for the alpha asshole museum. And, the book was 1,400 pages on my e-reader. That's a long time to hate someone. I think my blood pressure took a hit during this reading. I need wine.<br/><br/>Okay, so we have Violet, a widow with two teenage daughters, and Joe, an asshole who lives next door. They have a not-so-nice meeting where Joe acts like a total jerk. Later, he comes up to her at the local bar while she's drunk</span>
  <span id="freeText2179646783553414280" style="display:none">Just shoot me. This fucking book! I wanted to murder the main guy. He is an alpha asshole for the alpha asshole museum. And, the book was 1,400 pages on my e-reader. That's a long time to hate someone. I think my blood pressure took a hit during this reading. I need wine.<br><br>Okay, so we have Violet, a widow with two teenage daughters, and Joe, an asshole who lives next door. They have a not-so-nice meeting where Joe acts like a total jerk. Later, he comes up to her at the local bar while she's drunk and decides to take advantage of that fact. You know how you read these romances and the lead male character is all noble and shit and refuses to sleep with the drunk girl? Yeah, this guy isn't noble at all. Even when she says she's not on the pill, and he doesn't have condoms, he says, "Fuck it" and has sex with this drunk woman who can barely stand up anyway. <br><br>What a hero! How romantic! Isn't he awesome?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463339804i/19107864.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After a couple of nights of booty calls, he cuts her loose in the most humiliating way possible. After this happens, she avoids him - you know, like a normal human would do. And, she's pissed off - again, a human-like reaction. So, good old Joe calls her a bitch. Yup, he's that awesome. I know what you are thinking, girls, "Where can I find a great guy like this?" I'm thinking you can go to any prison or biker bar and find guys of this caliber.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463339804i/19107865._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>This guy might be available. And, he's better than Joe.</i><br><br>So, Violet moves on and meets another guy, Mike. Mike is normal. He asks her on a date. He gives her time to see where her head is at. He treats her with decency and doesn't even cuss her out. What a loser!! So, of course she goes back to screwing Joe. <br><br>They've got a great situation worked out. Mike takes Violet out on nice dates and drops her off at home with a goodnight kiss, then she goes over to Joe's house and has sex with him. Joe is cool with this arrangement. He doesn't have to do the work, but gets the payoff. Violet is cool with this. She's obviously a low-class slut. Mike.... well, Mike doesn't actually know about this. What Mike doesn't know won't hurt him, right?<br><br>So, at this point I'm thinking Violet deserves Joe. They are both a couple of assholes.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463339804i/19107866._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Two for one special here!</i><br><br>Aside from the horrible horrible couple in this book, it was also just waaaay too long. It dragged on and on with angst and break-ups and fights and dramatic bullshit until I wanted to burn the world down just to get rid of this book. Seriously. I considered the Witness Protection Program to get out of this buddy-read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463339804i/19107867._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But, my friends at BBB make the torture of these KA books worth it, so of course I will be ready for our next book. I'm such a masochist!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer471995209" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5090205477667426775"><b>This was a Buddy re-read with Alleskelle and Irene. This book is perfection. I used think Tate was my number one KA hero but Joe "Cal" Callahan has toppled him. There are tears, laughter, suspense, teenagers, dogs, drinks, food. It has it all. HIGHLY RECOMMEND THIS.</b><br/><br/>Decided to do a re-read. Was it as good the second time around – even better…..<br/><br/>Sexy Joe Callahan …<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391027474i/8319090._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380735648i/3116842.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>He was a dick, Christ he was a dick, he should cut her loose. For the life of him, he just fucking couldn’t.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400031i/774688.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>Loved the way poor Vi was ca</span>
  <span id="freeText5090205477667426775" style="display:none"><b>This was a Buddy re-read with Alleskelle and Irene. This book is perfection. I used think Tate was my number one KA hero but Joe "Cal" Callahan has toppled him. There are tears, laughter, suspense, teenagers, dogs, drinks, food. It has it all. HIGHLY RECOMMEND THIS.</b><br><br>Decided to do a re-read. Was it as good the second time around – even better…..<br><br>Sexy Joe Callahan …<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391027474i/8319090._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380735648i/3116842.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>He was a dick, Christ he was a dick, he should cut her loose. <span id="freeTextContainer1938386870473916952"><br/>This was my umpteenth reread! This was the 9th time I read it (I KNOW, RIGHT?!?!?!) and I already want to read it again. Perhaps I have issues or maybe it's because<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380893795i/3144154.jpg' alt=' photo myheartbelongstojoe_zps0cf2051d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Do I think Joe Callahan is the ultimate alpha created by Kristen?? Well ... DUH!<br/><br/>You know how we all have this one book that we find perfect for one reason or another. This is <b>MY</b> perfect book. It's</span>
  <span id="freeText1938386870473916952" style="display:none"><br>This was my umpteenth reread! My ultimate favorite read of Kristens!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418414340i/12781512.jpg" alt=" photo 2b892c54-33c6-42b0-874e-7659bcdc8aec_zps5fad62ab.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I have a confession to make ... this is the most read book on my Kindle and my absolute KA favorite. This was the 9th time I read it (I KNOW, RIGHT?!?!?!) and I already want to read it again. Perhaps I have issues or maybe it's because<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380893795i/3144154.jpg" alt=" photo myheartbelongstojoe_zps0cf2051d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do I think Joe Callahan is the ultimate alpha created by Kristen?? Well ... DUH!<br><br>You know how we all have this one book that we find perfect for one reason or another. This is <b>MY</b> perfect book. It's always a sure cure for my book slumps! <br><br>What I love about this book is absolutely<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420970i/835822.jpg" alt=" photo everything_zpsfb8187da.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story (I am sure you read the synopsis so I won't bother with it) is perfection! Even the one and only part that bothers me every time I read this book (where Mike tells Vi the story that isn't his to tell!) I have managed to come to terms with ... somewhat.<br><br>Now onto the best parts of the book ...<br><br>Joe Callahan ...*sigh*... what can I say other than <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380896053ra/3144753.gif" alt=" photo cantstoplovingyouarrow_zps64fbd9ce.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Joe/Cal</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800947i/677258.jpg" alt=" photo joecalatpeace_zpsa403f0e0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know many viewed him as asshole for the first 45% of the book due to some of his actions but I just don't see it. Sorry, ladies and gents! We all have reasons for doing things we do and I think Joe's were pretty valid ones. Was he not always honest/upfront about what he wanted?? Then what more do you want from a guy??<br><br>Then there is Violet a.k.a. Vi and/or "buddy" ...<br><br><b>Vi/"buddy"</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412977i/812543.jpg" alt=" photo ViAtPeace_zps4ee7c31b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Usually I want to bitchslap a heroine at least once in most books I read. Vi managed to sail through the entire story without getting on my nerves even a little bit ... She is such a great character! A perfect combination of sweet/a little bit naive and strong/loyal. Reading about her with her girls was one of the sweetest things ever!<br><br>And speaking of the girls ...<br><br><b>Keira and Kate</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380899043i/3145622.jpg" alt=" photo kateandkeiraatpeace_zps43918485.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>are probably the cutest teenage duo I've ever read about. The way they took to Joe and he to them ...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380847637ra/3133582.gif" alt=" photo swooning_zps71b5f5d6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Scratch my above statement about Vi with her girls being one of the sweetest things I've ever read about ... Joe with the girls was equally as sweet if not sweeter!<br><br><br>All in all, this is a great book that will make you laugh and it will make you cry. The story is one of the most heartwarming stories KA has ever written, IMO. I just love when a big, strong, ÜBER MACHO guy tries to fight (to no avail!) his feeling &amp; then finally succumbs to those feelings only to become THE ultimate book boyfriend we all wish for IRL!<br><br><br>An absolute MUST for any KA fan and everyone else in between!<br><br><br>*** This is also a fantastic book for a <b>BUDDY</b> read ;) which I've done on numerous occasions with some of my favorite GR "buddies" (Kim and Jennifer being the two).</span>

<div id="review_535413673" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/535413673" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/535413673?book_show_action=true">Feb 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/31361816-at-peace">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-series">cont-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=a-re-read">a-re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=kristen-ashley">kristen-ashley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer535413673" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3089243589007006513">Still bloody brilliant.<br/><br/>One of my all-time favourite Kristen Ashley reads/listens. There are so many things that I feel I could hold against Joe but by the end, you can't help but love him. His relationship with Kate and Keira always makes me smile as he steps into their lives so effortlessly. Cradling them in his arms when they face heartbreak could make anyone's heart melt.<br/><br/>It's sexy, emotional and it's enthralling. I will be back again...soon...ish. :-)<br/><br/>**********<br/><br/><b>Baking can be very, very emotion</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3089243589007006513" style="display:none">Still bloody brilliant.<br><br>One of my all-time favourite Kristen Ashley reads/listens. There are so many things that I feel I could hold against Joe but by the end, you can't help but love him. His relationship with Kate and Keira always makes me smile as he steps into their lives so effortlessly. Cradling them in his arms when they face heartbreak could make anyone's heart melt.<br><br>It's sexy, emotional and it's enthralling. I will be back again...soon...ish. :-)<br><br>**********<br><br><b>Baking can be very, very emotional...</b><br><br><i>An Audio Review</i><br><br>How’s my form…baking cookies and cupcakes with tears pouring out of my eyes. Hubby walks past and doesn’t even ask if I’m OK? He just shakes his head and keeps on walking. I mean, I could have burnt myself, be recovering from a concussion after slipping in egg whites or sprained my wrist with all of the mixings with a hand mixer. I’ve been hinting to hubby I need a Kitchenaid stand mixer. I have this one recipe for coconut cookies that you have to beat for 5 minutes, my arms feel like they’re going to fall off by the end. Anyways… Noooo, he just walks on by. To be honest, he knows me too well. The bugger knows I get a wee bit emotional when I’m living in KA world.<br><br>So I’ve read <i>At Peace</i> a few times, absolutely love the highs and low of Joe and Vi’s journey. When the audio went on sale for $1.99 (that price is from Audible if you own the Amazon ebook already) I snapped that sucker up. I started hesitantly after some complaints that the narrator was quite monotone, but that wasn’t my complaint. I could hear swallowing…I hate that in real life let alone right in my ear. It wasn’t throughout the whole book but it did happen. So was it worth $1.99? Too bloody right :-)<br><br>Vi and her two daughters Kate and Keira, have moved to The Burg trying to get away from a madman who killed her police officer hubby. The mad man has the hots for Vi and wants her. Unfortunately, she didn’t get far enough away. He finds her and starts harassing her again. Lucky for Vi she moved in across from Alex (Burg police) and Feb Colton, and next door to security specialist Joe Callahan. The first time Joe and Vi meet isn’t ideal, but they feel an instant attraction to each other. Joe has issues and I mean serious ISSUES. This is the journey two people make to find happiness.<br><br>Unfortunately, the journey is fraught with barriers…mostly made by Joe. His issues date back 17 years and he still hasn’t gotten over them. What starts off as the two of them finding mutual satisfaction in each other's arms, becomes more for Vi. Vi’s husband was her first love and she doesn’t have a lot of experience, especially handling no strings attached sex. When Joe sees Vi getting attached to him, he does some very horrible things to make it clear that he’s not in the same headspace. There are more casualties, though…Joe started a friendship with Vi’s teenage daughters. One other issue, when Vi tries to move on, she starts a more “normal” relationship with Mike a detective in the Burg. It’s not great…and she does keep them both on the line…I can only blame her inexperience.<br><br>Not saying anymore…I’ve probably said too much already. But I wanted to make clear that even though Joe does some really douchey things…when he comes good he comes really, really good. That brings us to another point. This man is HOT!! I mean he takes her to market, he takes her at home, he cooks her beef on the barbie and makes sure Tina has none, And then Joe gives her O’s O’s O’s all the way home.<br><br><a href="http://staceyissassy.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440643271i/16004133._SX540_.jpg" width="300" height="48" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/StaceyisSassy" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004243.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/Stacey1565/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004244.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.twitter.com/StaceyisSassy" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440644070i/16004245.jpg" width="40" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a></a></span>
  <a data-text-id="3089243589007006513" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1972748332" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5630845385799456904"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally read 4/16/2017)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4 Stars <i>(Re-Read 2/11/2019)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4 Stars<i>(2nd Re-Read 12/2/2019)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 3.5 Stars <i>(3rd Re-Read 10/12/2020)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Re-Read Update:</b> This was an enjoyable re-read. I'm going to keep my rating the same. I did have some issues with the h leading on Mike while still emotionally attached to Joe, but I also understood what she was doing (and Mike knew what she was doing). There were some moments where I felt the length of the book. I never skimmed, but it felt <i>long</i>. I also felt like that</span>
  <span id="freeText5630845385799456904" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally read 4/16/2017)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4 Stars <i>(Re-Read 2/11/2019)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4 Stars<i>(2nd Re-Read 12/2/2019)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 3.5 Stars <i>(3rd Re-Read 10/12/2020)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Re-Read Update:</b> This was an enjoyable re-read. I'm going to keep my rating the same. I did have some issues with the h leading on Mike while still emotionally attached to Joe, but I also understood what she was doing (and Mike knew what she was doing). There were some moments where I felt the length of the book. I never skimmed, but it felt <i>long</i>. I also felt like that ending was a total let down and not at all up to par for what I come to expect out of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> books. <br /><br /><b>2nd Re-Read Update:</b>Nothing really to add here -- still bugged about Mike, still felt a little too long at times, and the ending still let me down...but! I like these characters and their story enough to keep my rating at 4 stars.<br /><br /><b>3rd Re-Read Update:</b> Same issues as before, but seemed to lag a little bit more and didn’t quite pack the emotional punch as it previously had. Very well could be the fact that I’ve re-read this so many times, or it could be simply attributed to my book funk 🤷🏻‍♀️<br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was cute! I'm not quite sure why, but I haven't been all that interested in this series -- but I'm glad I gave it a shot! I enjoyed both of the main characters, and I loved the H's interactions with the h's daughters (something KA always seems to get right IMO)! I also got that town/family feel that I love in KA books here. Both Joe and Violet's pasts broke my heart, but it just made me root for their happiness so much more! BUT -- I would've loved to see a farther glimpse into their HEA though! Yes. I am a greedy, greedy girl ;). It also dragged a little here and there to where I think some of the unimportant stuff could've easily been edited out. But, all in all -- I enjoyed it and it's going in my mental log of KA successes!<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Violet and Joe's story. Violet lost her policeman husband and she needed a new start with her two teenage daughters, so she moves to the 'Burg. She finally meets her new mystery neighbor one night, and they are instantly attracted to each other. They bump into each other a few more times, but then start a hot casual affair. Joe isn't one for relationships, so he continues to push Violet away even though he also keeps wanting her. They are connected when some tragic events come to Violet and her family, and Joe goes fully in with his pursuit of Violet. There are some sad and funny moments, some sexy times, some suspense...and they get a HEA.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Violet and Joe's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Ok. As with most of KA's books, this was a little long. I actually felt it in this one too. I think it could've been edited down a bit to fully keep my interest. I never skimmed, but it did feel like it dragged in certain parts.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No, they take a while to develop stronger feelings.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Joe. I liked him. I understood his damage and I felt for his loss, but I really wanted to shake him a few times!<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Violet. I liked her. I did wish that she didn't fall under Joe's sexy spell as easily at times though ;)<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Moderate. There is a few scenes that had me crying, but never ugly crying.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H runs hot and cold. He has been majorly burned in the past, and is unsure of what he really wants, so he pushes her away at times. The H is the main pursuer of the relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Hot. They have some hot tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Condoms are not used. The h says she's not in birth control, but then gets on it. I don't remember any mention of std statuses or previous practices.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The h dates OM while being in pseudo-relationship with the H. The H's ex wife shows up and causes some drama at one point. The H makes the h think he slept with OW to push her away at one point. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I wouldn't call it descriptive, but there is a mention about what went down with the OM before she was with the H in a memory type inner thought. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b>Not technically, but kind of. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The h is an on-again-off-again non-defined relationship with the H when she gets with OM. She tells the OM, but I feel like she crossed some lines into cheating at times (especially with what I consider emotional cheating - on both the H and OM). There was mention that she had oral sex with OM, but it wasn't descriptive. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated a few times. The H wasn't with anyone else (does kiss OW in front of h and lies to her that he slept with this OW), but the h was with the OM (never intercourse, but as much as oral sex)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Loss of a spouse (h - off page), loss of a sibling (h - on page), violence/murder (on and off page), h has 2 daughters with dead husband, H is divorced, loss of a child and parent (H - off page), drug/alcohol abuse (side character - off and on page), and stalking/kidnapping (on page).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had alright closure with a cute jump ahead epilogue and a HEA ending. I still would've liked a farther jump ahead epilogue...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[to experience the blended family and Joe officially becoming a dad again <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I got it in loan through my public library.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one is probably either <u>Safe with exception</u> or <u>Not Safe</u> depending on personal preferences.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does </b> have cheating IMO (see above)<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM <br />- <b> Does</b> have the H pushing the h away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a few separations between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_427736890" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/427736890" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/427736890?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Stacia (the 2010 club) by: </span>
      Buddy read with Sea and all of the AA peeps
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=suspense-or-thriller">suspense-or-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=slow-as-molasses">slow-as-molasses</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer427736890" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17675431022933517170"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Dear Goodreads Friends,<br/><br/>I'm sorry to have to go against the trend here, but I can't seem to wrap my mind around a 1,000 plus page contemporary romance book. Someone please come let me know if Ms. Ashley ever decides to write one in about half of the space and I might be willing to check it out. Thanks.<br/><br/>Your Exasperated Friend,<br/>Stacia XOXOXO</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>I do think there was a good story buried among the rubble of excess character description, shopping scenes, and the home and garden report. However, </span>
  <span id="freeText17675431022933517170" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Dear Goodreads Friends,<br /><br />I'm sorry to have to go against the trend here, but I can't seem to wrap my mind around a 1,000 plus page contemporary romance book. Someone please come let me know if Ms. Ashley ever decides to write one in about half of the space and I might be willing to check it out. Thanks.<br /><br />Your Exasperated Friend,<br />Stacia XOXOXO</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />I do think there was a good story buried among the rubble of excess character description, shopping scenes, and the home and garden report. However, my patience isn't up for reading page after page of gossip about who is who at the BBQ, what Mike's house looks like on the inside, and how much care and attention Vi put into her backyard. When a 'random' scene having nothing to do with the actual story drags on for pages, my eyes start to glaze over.<br /><br />This is contemporary romance (w/a side of suspense) - not the type of story which requires a lengthy word count, such as a high fantasy or historical fiction might in some instances.<br /><br /><b>What I did like about this story :</b><br /><br />~ The Characters. I didn't struggle with Joe or Vi the way that some other people did. I didn't care that Vi hooked up with more than one man (guys do it all the time, after all...turnabout is fair play). The daughters were cute and fun to read about, although somewhat unrealistic sounding. I'm around teens constantly, and none of them sound like these girls. <br /><br />~ The Chemistry. Joe and Vi had great chemistry and the sex was enjoyable to read. Almost all of the scenes involving Joe and Vi or Joe with the family were worth reading. <br /><br />I am always a sucker for men who want to own their women in the bedroom : <i>He ground his cock in deep and demanded, "Who do you belong to?"</i><br /><br />~ The "scales" storyline. All of the dialogue involving the scales and weights was endearing and heartwarming.<br /><br /><b>What I didn't like about this story :</b><br /><br />~ Mike's part in all of this. I have seen this pattern before with KA books. One of the heroes falls for the leading lady and she rejects him, so he gets a chance for his own book later. Eh...I find this method unnecessary. There are other ways to introduce a future character. Let him be the lonely neighbor who is closed off to the world, so we're all curious to know more about who he is.<br /><br />~ Editing issues. This is nothing new. FFS, passed and past do not mean the same thing. <br /><br />~ As mentioned before - it was too long. I would also mention that there are too many characters. If we're introducing characters for future books, then it's probably better that we meet one or two at a time in each book, not 10 (or so) of them in one book.<br /><br />~ The obligatory love/drug reference. As if I'd miss this in any book. <i>Shit, he was like a drug and I realized I'd been jonesing for him all day.</i><br /><br />~ The obligatory nicknames. Does every single book need to have nicknames? Is this a trademark? If so, can we get something other than BUDDY?!? Really...BUDDY?!? If some guy called me that, I'd hurt him. This ties with Daddy for being on the list of worst nicknames ever.<br /><br />~ Other than the Italian family, everyone sounded the same. Again, another recurring issue with KA books. In real life, not all men sound the same, not even if they're all alpha. So why does every man (and even an occasional woman) in these books (from various ethnic/cultural backgrounds and locations) sound like they all grew up in the same 2 block radius?<br /><br /><b>Case in Point :</b><br /><br /><i>Joe -</i> "I'm not leavin' for two weeks not gettin' my fill of you."<br /><br />"Buddy, you want me fuckin' you with your girls in the house then you stay home. You don't, I hear your feet on the steps of my deck."<br /><br />"Split you in two, I fuck you harder."<br /><br /><i>Mike -</i> "You're comin' to my house. I'm makin' you dinner."<br /><br /><i>Sam -</i> "I'd hate to see you sittin' there, glarin' at me while I'm eatin' it. Shit's fuckin' ambrosia."<br /><br /><i>Tina -</i> "Know you walked out Cal's backdoor wearin' his shirt. Know you're stringing' along a good man like Mike. Know that's fucked."<br /><br /><b>This author has the ability to deliver on great characters and story, if only she'd mix it up more with each book.</b> I'd love to see some beta males, or at least an alpha who isn't the same controlling (yet lovable) jackass. If she could figure out how to make each book stand alone as something completely unique from the last book and work on possibly condensing and editing, then I really do think we might be looking at something great. I'm hoping that someday I'll find the KA book which truly works for me. I'd love to be able to give one of her books a rating higher than 3 stars because I see what could be. We're just not there yet. <br /><br />I had officially decided to take a break from KA books after Motorcycle Man, but this was a buddy read that I was talked into by a good friend who I simply couldn't say no to. I'm not sorry that I read the book because I did enjoy it in parts, even with my complaints. However, this will be my "official" time now to break from this author for a good, long while. You might see me read another KA book someday, when my memory is at least slightly fuzzy from my last read, so I'm not comparing details too closely in my head. <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17675431022933517170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer285003120" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5938126196225937148"><br/><b>Awesome!!!! Kindle Price Drop!<br/><br/>Gearing up for Frankie and Benny's story!</b><br/><br/>The first 4 books in the series are only $1.99 for a limited time!<br/><br/><b>#1 - For You -</b> <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/For-You-Burg-Series-ebook/dp/B004S81POK/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&ie=UTF8&qid=1378830879&sr=1-1'>http://www.amazon.com/For-You-Burg-Se...</a><br/><br/><b>#2 - At Peace - </b><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Peace-The-Burg-Series-ebook/dp/B004Z1GHG6/ref=sr_1_2?s=digital-text&ie=UTF8&qid=1378830879&sr=1-2'>http://www.amazon.com/Peace-The-Burg-...</a><br/><br/><b>#3 - The Golden Trail - </b><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Golden-Trail-Burg-Series-ebook/dp/B005AU8KM0/ref=sr_1_3?s=digital-text&ie=UTF8&qid=1378830934&sr=1-3'>http://www.amazon.com/Golden-Trail-Bu...</a><br/><br/><b>#4 - Games of the Heart - </b><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/Golden-Trail-Burg-Series-ebook/dp/B005AU8KM0/ref=sr_1_3?s=digital-text&ie=UTF8&qid=1378830934&sr=1-3'>http://www.amazon.com/Golden-Trail-Bu...</a><br/><br/>---------<br/><br/><i>At Peace</i> has become one of my very favorite Kristen Ashley books, and Joe Callahan has become my favorite, most o</span>
  <span id="freeText5938126196225937148" style="display:none"><br /><b>Awesome!!!! Kindle Price Drop!<br /><br />Gearing up for Frankie and Benny's story!</b><br /><br />The first 4 books in the series are only $1.99 for a limited time!<br /><br /><b>#1 - For You -</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/For-You-Burg-Series-ebook/dp/B004S81POK/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1378830879&amp;sr=1-1">http://www.amazon.com/For-You-Burg-Se...</a><br /><br /><b>#2 - At Peace - </b><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Peace-The-Burg-Series-ebook/dp/B004Z1GHG6/ref=sr_1_2?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1378830879&amp;sr=1-2">http://www.amazon.com/Peace-The-Burg-...</a><br /><br /><b>#3 - The Golden Trail - </b><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Golden-Trail-Burg-Series-ebook/dp/B005AU8KM0/ref=sr_1_3?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1378830934&amp;sr=1-3">http://www.amazon.com/Golden-Trail-Bu...</a><br /><br /><b>#4 - Games of the Heart - </b><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Golden-Trail-Burg-Series-ebook/dp/B005AU8KM0/ref=sr_1_3?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1378830934&amp;sr=1-3">http://www.amazon.com/Golden-Trail-Bu...</a><br /><br />---------<br /><br /><i>At Peace</i> has become one of my very favorite Kristen Ashley books, and Joe Callahan has become my favorite, most over the top, nigh unto Neanderthal, über alpha heroes ever. Mitch Lawson still holds the #1 spot for favorite, most realistic, über alpha hero from Kristen Ashley’s books, but yeah… Cal is everything I love in a tormented hero and there’s no question in my mind that if I could choose a hero to bring home and love all better, it’d be Joe.<br /><br />From the first page to the last, <i>At Peace</i> brings so much heartache, so much family drama, and yet, so much hope, humor, passion, love and devotion… I can’t remember how many times I was in tears, but it was often. Vi and her daughters, Kate and Keira, are awesome, and then with Sam, Mel, Bea, Gary, Pete, Vinnie, Theresa… we got an incredible supporting cast who I loved getting to know, as well as revisiting with many of the folk from <i>For You</i> . And Tim… wow… even in death he had a powerful presence and I loved getting to know him, and mourned him as though he’d been right there all along. But then again, in ways he <i>was.</i><br /><br />The bottom line – Time and time again, Kristen Ashley has given me stories I can immerse myself in, characters I can believe in, and she has given me hours and hours of absolute reading pleasure. As with most of her books, the page count is huge, and yet, never enough.<br /><br />-----<br />If you're a Kristen Ashley addict, or just interested in checking her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads! <br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_291644283" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/291644283" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/291644283?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of alpha heroes</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Auntee by: </span>
      All my GR friends
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=for_my_kindle">for_my_kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2012_reads">2012_reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=made_me_cry">made_me_cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=keepers">keepers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer291644283" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2623893253842820874"><i>Joe Callahan, also known as "Cal", minus the scars that mar his gorgeous face....</i><br/><a href='http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&current=joe-francescocura-1.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379768588i/269378.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>So I'm sitting here, stalling, wondering how to convey my thoughts about this one. So many people have raved about this author, and finally, after a few not-so-gentle nudges, I decided to give KA a try. And oh boy, I've boarded the KA train, and I'm afraid I don't want to get off! I haven't picked up another book since I've finished this one days ago. I just can't get over security expert Joe and his next-door-n</span>
  <span id="freeText2623893253842820874" style="display:none"><i>Joe Callahan, also known as "Cal", minus the scars that mar his gorgeous face....</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=joe-francescocura-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379768588i/269378.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So I'm sitting here, stalling, wondering how to convey my thoughts about this one. So many people have raved about this author, and finally, after a few not-so-gentle nudges, I decided to give KA a try. And oh boy, I've boarded the KA train, and I'm afraid I don't want to get off! I haven't picked up another book since I've finished this one days ago. I just can't get over security expert Joe and his next-door-neighbor Violet (okay, who am I kidding, it's <i>Joe</i> that I can't get over!) But how to explain how this story totally captivated me? It wasn't a flawless book by any means. And by that I'm not only talking about some weirdly structured sentences, a few grammatical mistakes, and a couple of slow passages that could've used some editing-- I'm talking about the main characters. Joe/Cal, 39, was not your perfect romance hero--he was a dominant alpha male, rude, crude, not much of a talker or communicator, (except when he wanted sex), and at times I was very ticked off with the way he treated Vi (or "Buddy" as he liked to call her) <i>and</i> I thought he didn't treat women (or think of them) with a whole lot of respect. I understood that his years spent <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ with his doozy of a first wife and the tragedy in their life <i>really</i> messed him up emotionally, but c'mon Joe, it was 17 years ago. Time to get back on the horse and give a real relationship another try, or get some therapy already! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But something about the way he took control of Vi, like he couldn't get enough of her and became out of control...boy that was hot. So yeah, the fact that he <i>wasn't</i> perfect made him a much more interesting character and really worked for me!<br><br><i>"And then there were his eyes. Sky blue eyes.</i> Sky. <i>F***ing</i>. Blue."<br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=francesco-cura.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380371945i/725085.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now the beautiful 35-year-old widow Vi, I liked for the most part. I liked that she was a hard worker, was able to overcome the terrible tragedy in her life, took care of her two teenage daughters, Kate and Keira (who were nicely drawn characters), and I enjoyed the inner dialogue she had with herself (especially regarding her feelings about Joe). I liked how she handled her relationship with Joe (most of the time). The one thing that I didn't like was how she treated Mike (the man who was also vying for her affections). I didn't like how she <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ kept him on a string while she tried to get over Joe. I couldn't believe <i>how far</i> she took the relationship! Yes, I realize Mike knew what he was getting into, being a rebound guy and all, but I think Vi had no business getting involved with him so soon. It just seemed a little selfish to me, and almost made me not like her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The best part of the book? The <b>smokin'</b>, and I mean <b>SMOKIN'</b> hot physical relationship between Joe and Vi. Joe was one big badass, an intense, <i>physical</i> lover, who kept Vi coming back for more (even when she knew she shouldn't!) Wow, Joe...just...wow. Mmmmmm....<br><br><i>Joe's classic Mustang starred in one memorable scene...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=joesmustang.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380371945i/725086.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>"You kiss me before you leave my house."</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=francesco_cura_200806_1-1-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380371945i/725087.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>"So, don't matter tomorrow morning you still think I'm a d***, 'cause now, even though you're drunk, I'm gonna take you inside and f*** you 'til you ache."</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=francesco_cura_200805_6-3-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800946i/677253._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>While the physical stuff was toe-curling and all, the emotional aspects of the Joe/Vi relationship is what really sold me, and had me reluctant to put my e-reader down. Joe and Vi's relationship was filled with ups and downs, break-ups and intensely passionate makeups. Joe thought he had nothing left to give a woman besides sex, and when Vi realized that he may be right and she was tired of expecting more from him, she had a terrific scene where she laid it on the line for him...<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>"You've shut yourself up for so long in this f***ing house with your tragic memories, you have no idea what's about to walk out your door. Kate, Keira and me, we could have plugged that hole. We could have filled you so full, you'd be bursting. We would have loved that chance. We'd have given everything we had, no matter the time that slid by, graduations, weddings, grandbabies, you'd have been a part of us and we'd have given everything we had to keep you so full, you'd be bursting."<br><br>"Joe," she whispered, "you let me walk out this door, you'll lose your chance."</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I absolutely loved this scene, and Joe's reaction. But boy did it make me sad.<br><br>My other favorite emotional scene, one in which a beloved character is tragically killed, and Joe is there for Vi and her daughters...<br><br><i>He was warm and strong and solid and big enough to surround us with all of that and we all needed it, we needed something to hold onto.<br>He could go away later.<br>And anyway, he would.</i><br><br>Well I could go on and on, giving up plenty of scenes that touched me emotionally. But I'm not going to do that. I'm just going to suggest that anyone who enjoys a tortured hero, a bad boy, a bad a**, a dominant lover who takes what he wants and then wants some more, a guy who takes no s*** from anyone, be they male <i>or</i> female...a guy who protects what's his and you'd better not mess with what's his...if you like a hero like that, then Joe Callahan is for you. And when Joe finally lets himself have what he fights against for most of the book, when he finally is "at peace", you're going to love the man that he becomes, the man that was buried deep for 17 years.<br><br><i>Joe, finally at peace and a much better, happy man...</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=francesco_cura12-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380371945i/725088.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If you haven't given this author a try yet, do yourself a favor and pick <i>something</i> from her extensive catalogue. Even though this is the second book of this particular series, it <i>can</i> be read as a stand alone (if you don't mind a few spoilers). I am so grateful to all my Goodreads friends for their reviews and suggestions...and once again I'm kicking myself for waiting so long to react to their suggestion! If you're looking for a book that will grab you emotionally, make you squirm and blush with the sheer audacity of some of Joe's actions and declarations, and have you rooting hard for the heroine to have another shot of happiness in her life, then this is the book for you. I think that now that I've gotten all that out of my system, I'm ready to move on to <i>another</i> Kristen Ashley book. My only concern is....how's she going to top <b>At Peace</b>? 5 stars</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2623893253842820874" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1386879783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13891996753505160800"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442613783i/16258594._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I've been on a Kristen Ashley audio binge lately. This audio was 23 hours long. I figured it would take me a month to finish but instead it took a week and half. I really enjoyed listening to this one but there were some minor things that the narrator did that took some time getting use to... such as her swallowing noise. At the beginning when she'd do it would distract me from the story. <br/><br/>I'm Team Joe now! He makes a great KA alpha male. Vi, on the hand, drove me nuts for a portion of this book </span>
  <span id="freeText13891996753505160800" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442613783i/16258594._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've been on a Kristen Ashley audio binge lately. This audio was 23 hours long. I figured it would take me a month to finish but instead it took a week and half. I really enjoyed listening to this one but there were some minor things that the narrator did that took some time getting use to... such as her swallowing noise. At the beginning when she'd do it would distract me from the story. <br><br>I'm Team Joe now! He makes a great KA alpha male. Vi, on the hand, drove me nuts for a portion of this book with her stringing along two guys. I'm glad to know the other guy has his own book later in this series.. <br><br>Overall, I'm glad I got to meet Joe Callahan. ♥<br><br><b>SERIES:</b> <br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10813480.For_You__The__Burg___1_" title="For You (The 'Burg, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1327337194s/10813480.jpg" alt="For You (The 'Burg, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
