    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_255326447" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/255326447" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/255326447?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer255326447" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12940831576279371024"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390921290i/8298349.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380366299i/718501._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> **SQUEEEEE** O.M.G what a SENSATIONAL book!!! My heart is filled to bursting here. Love love LOVE!! </b><br/><br/>This is a <i> gorgeous </i> book about a second chance at love, life, family and healing. Kristen Ashley never ceases to amaze me with utter brilliance of her books. Just one winner after another!! Damaged Alpha male hero, strong heroine, beautiful story... whats not to love??<br/><br/><blockquote>
<i> <b> "You're mine, the girls are mine. I'm stakin' my claim with you right now..."<br/><br/>"You're unbelievable," I snapped.<br/><br/>"I'm yours."<br/><br/>That</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText12940831576279371024" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390921290i/8298349.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380366299i/718501._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> **SQUEEEEE** O.M.G what a SENSATIONAL book!!! My heart is filled to bursting here. Love love LOVE!! </b><br><br>This is a <i> gorgeous </i> book about a second chance at love, life, family and healing. Kristen Ashley never ceases to amaze me with utter brilliance of her books. Just one winner after another!! Damaged Alpha male hero, strong heroine, beautiful story... whats not to love??<br><br><blockquote>
<i> <b> "You're mine, the girls are mine. I'm stakin' my claim with you right now..."<br><br>"You're unbelievable," I snapped.<br><br>"I'm yours."<br><br>That socked me in the gut... Taking advantage, his face dipped close and his hands curled around both sides of by head.<br><br>"First fuckin' time you smiled at me in my bed, that's when it happened," he murmered." </b></i> </blockquote><br><br>After her cop husband's brutal muder a year ago, Violet moved to the Burg with her two teenage daughters. One night, at 3:33am, she's tossing and turning in bed, unable to sleep because someone is blaring music. In a huff, she stomps out to figure out where its coming from and give whoever was playing it a piece of her mind when she meets Joe Callahan. He's big, tall, rugged, striking, scarred, gorgeous, blunt, badass, and Alpha-out-the wazoo! But he kind of acts like a bit of a jerk (though not in a way that'll make you hate him) and needless to say, despite her intense attraction to him, Violet pretty much dislikes him... though, not for long :P<br><br><blockquote>
<i> "Who's the big guy next door?"...<br><br>"Joe Callahan."<br><br>"Good neighbour to have."...<br><br>"Why?"<br><br>"Looks like he could crush a rock with his fist." </i> </blockquote><br>(teehee)<br><br>It was really heart breaking because you felt how strongly Vi missed her husband. Hell, after a few paragraphs, I missed him. He sounded like such a perfect KA man - gorgeous, caring, protective. And she's struggling and trying to start a new life - working as hard as she can to keep her and the girls afloat in the aftermath of such a senseless tragedy.<br><br>Joe's work takes him away a lot, but every time he's back, Vi and him have some sort of interaction. And so begins their on-and-off-ish, swoony-to-us yet perhaps frustrating-at-first-to-Vi relationship.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i> "You already think I'm a dick."<br><br>I felt my heart beat faster and I whispered. "Joe-"<br><br>Joe cut me off. "So don't matter tomorrow morning you still think I'm a dick, 'cause now, even though you're drunk, I'm gonna take you inside and fuck you 'till you ache." </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Seriously though, every time they met, even from their slightly rough start, I was grinning like an idiot and squeeing right out loud (often quite loudly).<br><br><blockquote>
<i> <b> "And I was in that truck with Joe Callahan. Joe Callahan who was scary and thrilling all in himself. He was more man than I'd ever know and I spent most of my adult life around cops. His maleness filled the cab, dangerous, assertive, assaulting my senses." </b></i> </blockquote><br><br>And they come together (hmm, meant literally and figuratively *winks*) FAST!!! This book differs from most KA books (except perhaps <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_" title="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Mystery Man</a>) in that the hero/heroine sleep together (or, I should say, have wild, rough, hard, passionate, crazy hot, sexy-as-hell, sex) very close to the start of the book. In this story, the sex (or, honestly I should say f*cking lol) happens first, and the relationship develops second. What they have is explosive, undeniable, and freaking H.O.T... and it doesn't stop... very soon she's spending every night in his bed.<br><br>But Cal has gone through something tragic in his past that makes him unable to establish a permanent emotional connection and give himself fully over to any relationship even if its what his heart wants and as soon as his feelings for her grow too strong, he breaks both their hearts by leaving and breaking off the relationship.<br><br>But when Vi's husband's murderer comes back on the radar with his creepy-stalker-eye set on Vi, that isn't something he can just stand by and do nothing about, so its up to him to do what he can to protect her and the girls, even though he has his work cut out for him to make her trust him again.<br><br><b> And so begins the beautiful craziness of this book - with a seriously SWOONY romance, crazy drunk ex's, crazy creepy murderer/stalkers, the crazy fun of 2 teenage daughters, the craziness of amazing neighbors and family... and as Vi learns to love again, and as Joe learns to trust again, they both learn to find healing, comfort, love and security in each other ... and an absolutely perfect happy ending :) *melt* *squee* *swoon* </b><br><br>Joe. Freaking. Callahan. *swoon* has definitely made my absolute top list of guys... lol, especially after he worked his issues out. It was so sweet and heart warming watching him struggle with his emotions, wanting more, but not trusting, trying to do right by Vi and her girls, trying to protect their family. He might be rough around the edges, but he sure-as-hell could be ridiculously sweet and thoughtful. He just had a lot of walls up, guarding himself against future hurt that might mirror a past he's spent 17 years trying to forget. And when his back story finally comes out, you get it. Its horrible, tragic, and made me cry. It totally explained his behavior, his attitude and his reluctance to get fully into a relationship.<br><br>And since their relationship wasn't clearly defined for a while, there is a bit of a love triangle thing going on for part of the story, but its always clear who ends up with who especially since the other guy is the hero of book 4 of this series :P ... but can I just say, that judging by his swooniness, book #4 is gonna ROCK!<br><br>Joe was just so damaged and totally Alpha, the perfect tortured badass bad boy. And once he figured all his stuff out and finally accepted that he couldn't ignore or deny what he and Vi had, he went all-out possessive claimy Alpha and stopped at nothing to prove his intentions, his love and his dedication to both her and her girls. Dear Lord, its hard for one heart to handle that much swoon!! *dreamy sigh*<br><br><blockquote>
<i> "Joe burst out laughing and I froze, listening to the richness of it. I wasnt even certain he </i> could <i> laugh. <b> He was my hot-as-shit, bad boy, player, next door, security to the stars booty call. He was a serious, scary, rugged, sinister, alpha male. </b> Men like that didn't </i> laugh." </blockquote><br><br>If you want a book with steam, this is it. Its is SMOKING HOT!!! The steamy fan-yourself hotness starts at about 8% of the book and pretty much never lets up, in fact it pretty much just builds as the emotional factor increases as the story progresses.<br><br>I have to say, the only thing I didn't really like was how he called her 'buddy' - that's just a little weird and not exactly hot to me. But hey, if that's my only possibly complaint about the book (and it is), I can definitely live with it.<br><br><b> This book really sneaks up on you. There were twists that had me rocking back and forth crying, some utterly <i> beautiful </i> scenes, epic badass moments... Loss. Healing. Betrayal. Trust. Family. Friendship. Loyalty. Bonding. Love. </b><br><br>Seriously. KA is a genius. The depth to which she just "gets" deep connections between friends, family, lovers, is just sensational. You can't help but feel totally connected to them, be totally sympathetic to them, and you end up knowing them so well and feeling for them so strongly that its hard to believe they are not real. She has a magical way with words. Speaks straight to your heart.<br><br>I thought it was so beautiful how Joe never tried to replace Tim (Vi's husband) either with Vi or the girls. He was something different. He was special. He loved them for who they were, not for who he wanted them to be to him. He really was Superman &lt;3<br><br>Joe and Vi had have their share of hotness and swoon, but they also had their share of of heartache, of mistakes, and of misunderstandings. Watching them work together to learn to trust each other and develop a functional relationship just melted my heart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i> "I'm gonna piss you off, honey, probably enough for you to want to leave. I've got a temper and so do you, we're gonna clash.... But... we've both learned, this, what we have it's worth getting over it.... I won't give up on you, Joe, I promise. I just need you to promise the same thing." </i>
</blockquote><br><br>This book really makes you FEEL!!! I had lots of misty eyes and several tears. Not just from a sad event, often just because the level of emotional I was feeling for a scene was just so strong, it overflowed.<br><br>Also, I loved how Colt and Feb (the hero/heroine of book #1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10813480.For_You__The__Burg___1_" title="For You (The 'Burg, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">For You</a>) were integrated into this story. They live on the same street as Joe &amp; Vi and we see them a lot. I love when an author doesn't forget about the beloved characters from previous books. Its so wonderful to see the development of their happily-ever-after, even if its from the outside.<br><br>And Oh. My. God, the ending is intense!! It starts building slightly sooner than the classic KA 90% mark and your heart just goes right in your throat. Its absolutely epic - filled with cops, mafia, stalkers, murders, kidnappings, plenty of badass... just totally epic, emotional and thrilling!! <br>*mega grin/squee*<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> "Semper <i> fuckin' </i> fi." </b>
</blockquote><br><br>LOVE LOVE LOVE this book!! If you haven't read it yet, GO GO GO!!!!! Get book 1 and join the swoon-fest. You won't regret it!<br><br><b> Rating: 5+++ STARS </b><br><br>See above for my casting choices :)<br><br>~~~~~~<br><br>And lastly, this is ONLY for those of you who have already read the book cuz it'll either not make sense or spoil something for you if you haven't, but can I just say how much I LOVED this quote: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <i> <b> "It was a shit time for you, the worst, but you were there and you saw 'em doin' it. They crawled into this same fuckin' bed with me, so did you, and when you did, you all became mine." </b></i>  *MEGA. FREAKING. SWOON*  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>****************************<br><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_262373900" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/262373900" />
    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/262373900?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=tortured-souls">tortured-souls</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=cruel-hero">cruel-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-characters">fabulous-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-hero">fabulous-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-heroine">fabulous-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer262373900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1735255163486725651"><b>4 1/2 to 5 stars</b><br/><br/>WOW! I loved this book! <br/><br/>I will admit to not fully enjoying the first half of the story because the hero was a complete and utter jerk, but the second half more than made up for it and shined brilliantly. <i>At Peace</i> made me laugh. It made me cry. It made me happy. It made me sad. It made me giddy. It also made me irate at times. However, <i>At Peace</i> is packed with so much heart and soul it's impossible not to get caught up in all its splendor.<br/><br/>I was captivated and enthralled by the mean</span>
  <span id="freeText1735255163486725651" style="display:none"><b>4 1/2 to 5 stars</b><br /><br />WOW! I loved this book! <br /><br />I will admit to not fully enjoying the first half of the story because the hero was a complete and utter jerk, but the second half more than made up for it and shined brilliantly. <i>At Peace</i> made me laugh. It made me cry. It made me happy. It made me sad. It made me giddy. It also made me irate at times. However, <i>At Peace</i> is packed with so much heart and soul it's impossible not to get caught up in all its splendor.<br /><br />I was captivated and enthralled by the meaningful and awe-inspiring relationship that developed between Joe Callahan and Violet Winters and her daughters, Kate and Keira. Joe needed them as much as they need him, and their relationship left an indelible impression on me.<br /><br />I am grateful I read reviews before starting this book. I knew what to expect, how the love triangle would play out, and how cruel the hero would be during the first half of the story. Had I not been prepared, my enjoyment of this book undoubtedly would have suffered, which would have been a shame considering the fact this book is simply wonderful. <br /><br />The only reason I dropped the rating a half star is because of the climax chapter near the end. It just didn't fit with the overall tone of the book. It had a heavy "cops and robbers" feel that didn't resonate with the rest of the story. This book is about family, healing, redemption, and love; and, frankly, the "cops and robbers" chapter did nothing to enhance the overall story. It only diminished it. Luckily, the epilogue brought everything back on track, giving me that heartwarming feeling that only Kristen Ashley can give.  <br /><br /><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1735255163486725651" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_314593174" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/314593174" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/314593174?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone who loves the alpha</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Duchess Nicole by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/13784133-ireneoust">~IreneOust~</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=ebooks-i-own-smashwords">ebooks-i-own-smashwords</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=favorites-of-all-time">favorites-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=dirty-talk">dirty-talk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=humorous">humorous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=recommendations">recommendations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=5-star-read">5-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-romantic-suspense">genre-romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer314593174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10617695471058899524"><b>
  <blockquote>”You two come with so much baggage, it's a wonder you don't get crushed. And that's the thing, neither of you did. And you found each other. It's time to unload that burden and find some joy.”</blockquote>
</b><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375387i/729934.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I rarely gush and swoon and giggle and lose my ever loving mind for a book. I should have known Kristen Ashley would bring out my inner teenage girl. Joe Callahan and Violet, even Mike and Vi's daughters Kate and Kiera...they all stole my heart. Their story made my emotions run a crazy obstacle course </span>
  <span id="freeText10617695471058899524" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>”You two come with so much baggage, it's a wonder you don't get crushed. And that's the thing, neither of you did. And you found each other. It's time to unload that burden and find some joy.”</blockquote>
</b><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375387i/729934.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I rarely gush and swoon and giggle and lose my ever loving mind for a book. I should have known Kristen Ashley would bring out my inner teenage girl. Joe Callahan and Violet, even Mike and Vi's daughters Kate and Kiera...they all stole my heart. Their story made my emotions run a crazy obstacle course before setting in on “ADORE”. <br><br><b>
  <u>MY SYNOPSIS:</u>
</b><br>Violet Winters moved to the 'Burg after the death of her husband. She and her two teenager daughters are doing the best they can to move on with their lives. Her husband, Tim, was a wonderful father and partner, and if they don't have him, at least they have wonderful memories. <br><br>One night, the house next door is suddenly blaring music for hours on end. Since the house has been empty for months, Violet tries to give her neighbor a pass. But after hours of losing sleep, a fuming Vi finally storms over to Joe Callahan's house, livid and fed up. This initial meeting between Joe and Vi is a great precursor for how the next few months go...it's volatile, it's scary, it's passionate, it's confusing as hell...but boy, does it get their blood flowing.<br><br>Joe Callahan is a security specialist for the stars. He may live in the Burg, but he's rarely home. A chance 3 a.m. meeting with his cute and sexy neighbor leaves him titillated and interested. But Joe doesn't DO relationships. Like, <u>ever.</u> Not since the tragedy of his younger years. Joe is the very definition of a loner, and he has no place for a woman, especially one with two beautiful, wonderfully quirky daughters, one who lights him up with a smile, and one who wants, expects, and deserves more than he is able to give.<br><br>But when Violet's secrets come out and she is put in danger, Joe's protective instincts come out. And he realizes that somehow, these three women have squirmed their way into his heart, where no one else has been for seventeen years. And once Joe lays down a claim, I can't imagine anyone who would get in the way.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375387i/729935.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book has lots of fun Kristen Ashley type inclusions such as: <br>An awesome group of zany, wacky, distinctly loyal girlfriends<br>Some competition for our heroine's affections...with a hottie who gets a future book<br>A scary dude who forces the hero to go into protective commando mode<br>Endearing secondary characters who give our heroine a platform to show her awesomeness<br>Super duper alpha male that you might want to castrate a few times throughout the story, but you'll be really glad you didn't<br><br><b>
  <u>MY THOUGHTS:</u>
</b><br>Hahahahahha!!! My thoughts...get ready for a gushfest. It's almost ridiculous how much I loved this book. I had heard, being a big KA fan, of Joe Callahan, for quite awhile, by so many friends....but I've saved and savored her books like fine chocolate...little bits at a time. Partly because I can only take so much of her uber alpha, overbearingly bossy men, and partly because I'm attempting to prolong the end of her long list of amazing stories. <br><br>I.<br>Love.<br>Joe Callahan.<br><br>He is, without a doubt, one of the hardest of KA males to read about. Because for quite some time, he's a big fat jerk. No matter how hot and amazing he is, he does some really mean stuff to a woman that is extremely undeserving. <u>However,</u> he more than makes up for it, and you come to realize that Joe is in an even darker place than Vi is...he just hides it better. Joe's story is practically Burg lore, though, so Violet gets to know him more from the town gossip tree than she ever gets from him. Joe is secretive, a loner, and brusque to the point of rudeness. But he wants Violet. He wants her bad. Only, Violet doesn't like being played.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>”...if you're willing to help, I should take it. But I'm gonna tell you even though I figure you know, I think you're an asshole. I don't only not like you, I <i>hate</i> you. I <i>hate</i> how you played me. I <i>hate</i> that I was so fucking stupid, I let myself get played. I <i>hate</i> that you know about this because I <i>hate</i> that <i>you</i> know <i>anything</i> about <i>me</i>. And I <i>hate</i> that I have to accept help from you.” After she dealt her lethal succession of blows, she finished with, “But I'll do it...for my girls.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Poor, poor Violet. She's been so beaten down by life. Hard knock after hard knock should have left more than a mark on her heart...shouldn't someone with a story like this end up sad and broken? Not this chick! Vi still sees beauty in life, she has joy in her girls, she likes her job, and she's building a new life for herself and her daughters. There is a realism to Vi that makes me want to be her friend, and her life, full of money worries and teenage angst, jumps out at me from these pages. This story is full of REAL people, REAL life. Sexy neighbor Joe, no matter how big an ass, is also bringing out her sexuality again. And when Joe screws her...and decides to screw her over, she moves on to Mike, a town cop who is exactly the type of man that she should want. Mike and Joe begin to vie for her attention, and the sexy factor goes up a couple of notches.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>”She's sweet, she can be funny when she forgets to be sad. She's good to her girls, a great Mom and fuckin' gorgeous.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>One thing that I love about KA heroes is that they always see the value in a good woman. They always have a deeply hidden romantic nature that is not apparent at first. And when they finally accept that a woman is theirs, there is nothing that gets in their way...not even her! Call it stalking, call it an unhealthy obsession, these boys don't take no for an answer! And than goodness for that!!<br><br>So Joe is a broken man, but Vi brings out the happy Joe, and when this man gets romantic...SWOON!!!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>”Love it when you say my name, baby...The way you say 'Joe', every man would wish that was their name.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375387i/729936.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Not to mention the way that Joe is with Vi's daughters. I'm SUCH a sucker for a man who is good to kids. Joe come across as a natural father, and it's heart melting. These girls are dying for some stability, and Joe gives that to them...eventually. He also has to do a lot of questionable things to keep his girls safe, but it's all in the name of love. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>”Happy family and about fucking time.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>To sum it all up: Joe screws up more than any other KA alpha that I've read to date. This is probably not a good book to go into without prior knowledge of what it means to be a KA man. However, everyone makes mistakes, especially those of us with demons in our pasts. Joe...yeah, he makes a lot of mistakes. So does Violet. But this isn't just a romance. It's a <b>story</b>. It's not pretty. In fact, there are times that it's ugly. But in all, it's actually quite beautiful, because when it's all said and done...this Burg is going to have some happy, healthy couples.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10617695471058899524" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1114432626?book_show_action=true">Nov 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1114432626" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16772593306259300563"><b>5 give me more of that Joe STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417891294i/12590824.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re mine, the girls are mine. I’m stakin’ my claim with you right now and, you force it, I’ll do it with him too.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I'm repeating myself, but I just have to say it again...I kinda like to read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> books. I know you didn't expect that. ;D I'm so cheeky.<br/><br/>So, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11665750-at-peace' rel='nofollow noopener'>At Peace</a> is the second instalment in the The 'Burg Series and while I'm partial to the first book <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10813480-for-you' rel='nofollow noopener'>For You</a>, I still had to give this one 5 Stars just because anything less would have been</span>
  <span id="freeText16772593306259300563" style="display:none"><b>5 give me more of that Joe STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417891294i/12590824.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re mine, the girls are mine. I’m stakin’ my claim with you right now and, you force it, I’ll do it with him too.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I'm repeating myself, but I just have to say it again...I kinda like to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> books. I know you didn't expect that. ;D I'm so cheeky.<br><br>So, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11665750-at-peace" rel="nofollow noopener">At Peace</a> is the second instalment in the The 'Burg Series and while I'm partial to the first book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10813480-for-you" rel="nofollow noopener">For You</a>, I still had to give this one 5 Stars just because anything less would have been blasphemy. As always the writing is stellar, the characters are wonderful, lots of family drama, heartbreak and in this particular series the whole world created around the main players is just so rich and developed with a lot of care.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have some good and some very bad news for you:<br><br><u>good</u> -- I found the perfect man and you can read a whole book about him<br><br><u>bad</u> -- he is taken, or better yet he will be taken by the time you finish reading<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419781759ra/13125484.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh well, here is the story in a nutshell.<br><br>Widow and mother of two teenage kids, finds herself in a torrid affair with her next door neighbour.<br><br>Of course it's a lot more complicated and drama is strong in this one, but it's a good start. ;D<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So <b>Violet Winters</b>, said single mother of two teenage girls had lost her husband when he was killed by a crazy stalker mafia boss who has an insane obsession with Violet and wants her all to himself.<br><br>Yeah, you can already see this is one of those books. Bring the crazy from the get go, why don't you?<br><br>First and foremost Violet is a mother. Everything she does is for the well being and safety of her daughters, Kate and Keira. Especially after they lost their father. But then one night loud music coming out of her neighbour’s house leads her down a path of personal happiness and satisfaction. Woooop Woooop...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You already think I'm a dick.”<br><br>I felt my heart beat faster and I whispered. “Joe-”<br><br>Joe cut me off. “So don't matter tomorrow morning you still think I'm a dick, 'cause now, even though you're drunk, I'm gonna take you inside and fuck you 'till you ache.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Oh <b>Joe Callahan</b>, you awesome -- awesome man. *sigh*<br><br>One prime example for a real swoon worthy alpha male. He has it all; he is domineering, a little mysterious, gorgeous and he has the tragic past. What more can a girl hope for? Oh, I know...he loves Vi's kids. OMG, he might just be PERFECT! Damn you, Ms. Ashley!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really like Vi and Joe's story. From the start the two have some scorching chemistry and don't even get me started with explosions happening when they get together. SCORCHING!<br><br>But that doesn't mean everything is sunshine and daisies. Joe and Vi have to fight many obstacles starting with their own stupidity, Mike (I dislike this one the most), a murderous mafia boss and not to mention a gossiping town.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Worth the wait," Joe muttered and my head tipped back. <br>"What?" <br>"Every bit of it. Every day, every week, every year, every fuckin' second, buddy," he kept muttering, his eyes intense, his face serious and my breath caught, "this. All of it. Worth the wait.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>It took me weeks to write this review and I'm sorry it is rather short and surely not my best, but I had to write something. And I really wanted you to meet Mr. Callahan. <br><br>I hope you can forgive me. ;P<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <td colspan="2">

<span id="freeTextContainer12158880585884931279">5 stars after a re read.<br/><br/>I love this book.<br/><br/>It is truly truly beautiful!<br/><br/>Violet Winters has moved the The 'Burg after losing her cop husband to a crime lord, a crime lord who then took an interest in her, and "stalked" her for months.<br/><br/>She moves in next door to Joe Callahan.<br/><br/>At first, they get off on the wrong foot!<br/><br/><i>
  <b> Wasn't that just the shit of it? There I was, in my predicament and I had security to the fucking stars living next door and I hated him because he was a huge jerk </b>
</i><br/><br/>But they have an attr</span>
  <span id="freeText12158880585884931279" style="display:none">5 stars after a re read.<br /><br />I love this book.<br /><br />It is truly truly beautiful!<br /><br />Violet Winters has moved the The 'Burg after losing her cop husband to a crime lord, a crime lord who then took an interest in her, and "stalked" her for months.<br /><br />She moves in next door to Joe Callahan.<br /><br />At first, they get off on the wrong foot!<br /><br /><i>
  <b> Wasn't that just the shit of it? There I was, in my predicament and I had security to the fucking stars living next door and I hated him because he was a huge jerk </b>
</i><br /><br />But they have an attraction to each other, and both try to fight it, and even make a good go at fighting it, denying what they could mean to each other. There is hurt and hurtful words thrown on each side, but they cannot deny what they mean to each other.<br /><br /><i>
  <b> "You're unbelievable" I snapped.<br />"I'm yours"<br />That socked me in the gut, so hard it winded me and all I could do was stare up at him.<br />Taking advantage, his face dipped close and his hands curled around both sides of my head.<br />"First fuckin' time you smiled at me in my bed, that's when it happened," he murmured.<br />"Joe-"<br />"You're under my skin"<br />"Please-"<br />"I'm under yours"</b>
</i><br /><br />Not to say, Joe did not do some hurtful things, but it was all in an effort to protect himself, and once you know why he felt that need, your heart broke for him.<br /><br />But once he decided Violet was it for him, he was all there and completely committed to it.<br /><br />Add in some drama, a once again excellent set of secondary characters (and is it just me who wishes we could have had a lot more of Cal's secretary Lindy?") and you have a winner<br /><br />A beautiful heart wrenching 5 stars</span>

<div id="review_468579680" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/468579680" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/468579680?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24922638-at-peace">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=buddy-reads-are-the-best">buddy-reads-are-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=it-burns-us-precious">it-burns-us-precious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=jerk-of-my-dreams">jerk-of-my-dreams</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=best-of-the-best">best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=favorite-secondary-characters">favorite-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=indie">indie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=for-when-i-hate-everything">for-when-i-hate-everything</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer468579680" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer197776033931817737">When I was in college, I dated this guy who was . . . he really wanted to be a hardcore, badass kind of guy . . . but mostly he was just an ass. <br/><br/>He was my first serious boyfriend, and over the course of our relationship he got three tattoos. The first one was of the Chinese characters for . . . wait for it . . . "iron man." And trust me people, he was a big dude (6'4''), but "iron man" he was NOT. The second one was of a phoenix. In FLAMES. It was on the top of his arm with a rune that the guy a</span>
  <span id="freeText197776033931817737" style="display:none">When I was in college, I dated this guy who was . . . he really wanted to be a hardcore, badass kind of guy . . . but mostly he was just an ass. <br><br>He was my first serious boyfriend, and over the course of our relationship he got three tattoos. The first one was of the Chinese characters for . . . wait for it . . . "iron man." And trust me people, he was a big dude (6'4''), but "iron man" he was NOT. The second one was of a phoenix. In FLAMES. It was on the top of his arm with a rune that the guy at the tattoo place swore meant "unquenchable fire," but I'd never heard of that rune before or since, so I'm still skeptical, and then . . . the last one he got was of more Chinese characters . . . and this one (allegedly) meant . . . "unquestionable authority."<br><br>Like I said . . . an ASS.<br><br>And as hilarious as it is that there does indeed exist in this world a man with ALL THREE of those tattoos, that's not why I'm relating the shame of boyfriends-past. NOPE, I'm telling you this b/c I'm pretty sure ASS wanted to be Joe Callahan. <br><br>And maybe if he was, it would have worked out.<br><br>Scratch that, if he was Joe Callahan it would have <i>definitely</i> worked out.<br><br>"Who is Joe Callahan?" you ask, and I'll tell you: Joe Callahan is the only KA Alpha who (IMO) can give Luke Stark a run for his money (and not just b/c he doesn't have that godawful Luke-stache). <br><br><i>At Peace</i> is a VERY different kind of story than the first book in <i>The 'Burg</i> series, <i>For You</i>. It's still romantic suspense, and it's still dark and gritty, but this one not only has two precious teenage girls (who, depending on which one you get, call their mother either "Momalicious" or "Mawdy") to help lighten the overall mood, but the dark and gritty is tragic and personal rather than the relatively impersonal picking-off of February's ex-boyfriends. <br><br>Admittedly, it probably felt personal to Feb, but to us? Not really. We didn't know any of those guys. <br><br>But Violet . . . we know Violet. And we know Kate and Keira, her girls, so even if we don't know Tim (Violet's husband, and father of Kate and Keira), the fact that he was a cop who was killed by a mobster in Chicago . . . it <i>feels</i> more personal. <br><br>ESPECIALLY when the mobster who had Violet's husband killed has taken a shine to her (which is why she moved to the 'burg in the first place--to get her girls away from the creepy, stalker mob boss). <br><br>Guess how well that worked?<br><br>I'll give you a hint . . . not very. 'Cause this is KA y'all, and what kind of story would it be if moving away solved all of Vi's problems? Here's another hint: not much of one.<br><br>And who does Violet happen to move next door to in the the 'burg? Hmm?? <br><br>Joe Callahan, that's who.<br><br>And after they meet it's all hearts and flowers, right?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387492497ra/7606558.gif" width="349" height="199" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yeah, no.<br><br>But it gets there . . . eventually . . . <br><br>This is one of my all-time favorite KA books, and that's really saying something b/c KA&lt;-----I love her. Something about the combination of Violet and her girls and Joe . . . it's just . . . warm fuzzies, head to toe. Joe's this big, gruff guy who has NOT had an easy life, and it's made him hard. But these girls . . . turn him to GOO. And BONUS: no stupid tattoos. This really is a fantastic story, and about as likely to happen as any KA book (which is to say <i>un</i>likely), but it <i>is</i> the kind of modern day fairy tale that KA is so well-loved for. And guys, this entire series is still on sale for $0.99 each on Amazon, so get these suckers. If you already have them, get them for your sister (I did), or your best friend--It's what needs to happen. </span>
  <a data-text-id="197776033931817737" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6442219344313044764"><b>5 BEST-CUPPA-JOE-ON-THE-PLANET STARS!!!!!!</b><br/><br/>I didn’t expect this book to rip me apart. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380830610ra/3128116.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yes, it was unbelievably sexy and <b>HOLY CANNOLI JOE!!!!</b> The dirty talk is off the charts…but we’ll get to that… <br/><br/>Vi has been dealt a shit deal in life. She is a mother of two teenage girls….and a widow. After losing her husband a year and a half ago, she does what she has to do in order to get by. I loved loved loved her girls, Kate and Keira. They helped make this book for me. They made me laugh through the whole</span>
  <span id="freeText6442219344313044764" style="display:none"><b>5 BEST-CUPPA-JOE-ON-THE-PLANET STARS!!!!!!</b><br><br>I didn’t expect this book to rip me apart. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380830610ra/3128116.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, it was unbelievably sexy and <b>HOLY CANNOLI JOE!!!!</b> The dirty talk is off the charts…but we’ll get to that… <br><br>Vi has been dealt a shit deal in life. She is a mother of two teenage girls….and a widow. After losing her husband a year and a half ago, she does what she has to do in order to get by. I loved loved loved her girls, Kate and Keira. They helped make this book for me. They made me laugh through the whole book.<br><br><b>
  <i>I wondered why anyone on earth would need drugs. You could get high just having a family.</i>
</b><br><br>Joe is a man whore (Duh! Those are the best kind!). He and Vi are next door neighbors and end up using each other for sex. And it’s HOT!!! Any girl would take advantage of Joe. There’s a reason he is such an asshole. That reason split my heart into a million pieces.<br><br><b>My Joe:</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Sinister, rugged, interesting.<br><br>Like him? He’s Joe.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380754562i/3119908._SY540_.jpg" alt="Lucas Gil" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My Vi/Buddy:</b><br><br>Aka <b>

<div id="review_711704870" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/711704870" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/711704870?book_show_action=true">Sep 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer711704870" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14209258533984446835"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780787._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 5 BRILLIANT STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435529i/879914._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b><i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"I got older and that changed and all I wanted was a good woman and a family. All my life, with a slight variation on theme, that's all I ever wanted. Buddy, you've given me both. You think, givin' me that, I could </i> ever<i> balance those scales?" <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i></b>
</blockquote><br/>Oh <b>Joe Callahan</b>... How I <b>LOVE</b> you!! This guy... seriously... one of my all time favourite Kristen Ashley Alpha males. At fi</span>
  <span id="freeText14209258533984446835" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780787._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 5 BRILLIANT STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435529i/879914._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I got older and that changed and all I wanted was a good woman and a family. All my life, with a slight variation on theme, that's all I ever wanted. Buddy, you've given me both. You think, givin' me that, I could </i> ever<i> balance those scales?" <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i></b>
</blockquote><br>Oh <b>Joe Callahan</b>... How I <b>LOVE</b> you!! This guy... seriously... one of my all time favourite Kristen Ashley Alpha males. At first I thought he was a jerk. I was like, 'why do all these people like him so much?'. His fanclub was <b>HUGE</b>. Just when I thought I would be the minority and wouldn't love Joe like everyone did. We get his back story and my heart breaks so bad for him. No wonder he was such an asshole. He was broken by what happened and had pretty much given up on anything good ever coming his way. He didn't think he deserved happiness because he thought that what happened in the past was his fault. So he kept pushing Violet Winters, the widow next door with whom he has a sexual relationship with, away.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435529i/879915._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"What's beyond love?"<br><br>"Don't understand the question, Vi."<br><br>I didn't explain. Instead I said, "Whatever it is, that's what I feel for you." <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Violet Winters</b> suffered some tragedies of her own. The most recent being the death of her husband and highschool sweetheart, Tim. But what I loved about her was that she was able to pick herself up and move forward for her daughters. She was a great mother despite her own parents not being there for her when she got pregnant very young. She always tried to stay positive. When she meets Joe because of the loud music coming from his house, she is intantly attracted to him and scared of him. Still, she finds she wants to get to know him better, and find out why he is so alone. No matter how many times he pushed her away, she tried to break through his barriers so she could love him. Of course, Joe has to ruin it all so she gives up on him. Then Joe realizes that what he had and just let go of, he will never get again so he tries to get her back.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445492313ra/16660949.gif" width="400" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You're mine, the girls are mine. I'm stakin' my claim with you right now and, you force it, I'll do it with him too." <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Joe totally redeems himself! He made me swoon and sigh so hard. He was freaking perfect. I loved how alpha and protective he was with Vi. She was trying to move on with Mike but that didn't end up happening with how persistent Joe was to ger her back. But what totally won me was his interactions with Vi's daughters Kate and Kierra. OMG!! That was so beautiful to see. And the great thing was that these girls loved him back. There never resented him or ever thought he was trying to take their father's place. They welcomed him with open arms almost instantly. This was because they thought he was a good man for their mother, and they didn't want her to be alone anymore. Such amazing girls. I also loved that he wanted to show the girls that they deserved great guys who would appreciate them and nothing less. I loved that he was always there for Vi. Seriously... I love Joe.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I’m yours.”<br><br>That socked me in the gut too, so hard it winded me and all I could do was stare up at him. Taking advantage, his face dipped close and his hands curled around both sides of my head.<br><br>“First fuckin’ time you smiled at me in my bed, that’s when it happened,” he murmured. “You’re under my skin. I’m under yours.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/640155.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then came the scene that wrecked me. Vi suffers another tragedy that had me bawling!! My heart hurt, I couldn't believe it had happened. She had suffered enough. She went out of control and to be honest, I don't blame her. I probably would have reacted the same way. When I thought I couldn't possibly love Joe more, he shows up to offer his support to Vi and her daughters. I can't tell you how amazing that scene was. It was so weird how I felt so completely heart broken for what happened and yet, be so happy because of how wonderful Joe was. This was one of my favourite scenes in the book. Just because, it was beautiful seeing them altogether like that. Joe was an exceptional step-dad.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445492313ra/16660950.gif" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Every bit of it. Every day, every week, every year, every fuckin' second, buddy," he kept muttering, his eyes intense, his face serious and my breath caught, "this. All of it. Worth the wait." <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Overall, this book will be a part of my list of top best books by Kristen Ashley. I loved Joe. It was really emotional but there was some parts with humor and suspense that really grabbed your attention. I loved Joe. The sex was good and didn't overwhelm you. I loved Joe. All of the secondary characters were also really great. I really like how Kristen Ashley always provides a support system for the main characters. I loved Joe. I am really intrigued by Mike and I can't wait to read his story, as well as Benny's. I loved Joe. I definitely recommend you give this a read, especially if you love alphas because Joe won't disappoint. Oh, and before I forget, I really <b>LOVED</b> Joe. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14209258533984446835" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11286449622317177069"><b>**5++++ Just Amazing Stars**</b><br/><br/>Well I've added another KA alpha male to my book husband list. The sexy, dirty talking, slightly tormented, Italian (something about Italians that screams HOT!) loves with his whole heart Joe Callahan! I burned with heat for this man and he has my heart! Here's my banner for Joe:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438550910ra/15726935.gif' width='400' height='350' alt='description/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I love you KA for making such fabulous characters that make me swoon! I was like this the whole time:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423711391ra/13661892.gif' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And I'm sure Joe looks something like this:<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438551125ra/15726979.gif' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And yes <b>I'M IN LURVE!!</b><br/><br/>Violet had a crappy life, </span>
  <span id="freeText11286449622317177069" style="display:none"><b>**5++++ Just Amazing Stars**</b><br><br>Well I've added another KA alpha male to my book husband list. The sexy, dirty talking, slightly tormented, Italian (something about Italians that screams HOT!) loves with his whole heart Joe Callahan! I burned with heat for this man and he has my heart! Here's my banner for Joe:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438550910ra/15726935.gif" width="400" height="350" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I love you KA for making such fabulous characters that make me swoon! I was like this the whole time:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423711391ra/13661892.gif" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I'm sure Joe looks something like this:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438551125ra/15726979.gif" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And yes <b>I'M IN LURVE!!</b><br><br>Violet had a crappy life, her cop husband was shot dead by a lunatic who wanted her all to herself, but she kept strong. She takes care of her girls and everyone around her. She is simply a heroine <i>that didn't get on my nerves</i> and that in itself was a breath of fresh air! I loved how she kept calling herself a slut, because let's be honest she was acting like one but hey, who wouldn't be a slut when you're neighbor is thee Joe Callahan!! And that garage scene! *Fanning myself*<br><br>If you haven't read this, READ IT! This is KA at its finest.</span>
