<div id="review_243257819" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/243257819" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/243257819?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer243257819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6541454052498359216"><b>“Without peace of mind, life is just a shadow of its possibilities.” <br/>- by Jean Borysenko -<br/> <br/>3.5 stars.<br/> <br/>About my rating: Despite my issues it’s a well-written, emotional and engrossing story and therefore I rounded up to 4 stars.</b><br/><br/>Wow, deep breath...I know, I know, hold your horses, Baba! This was such an emotional rollercoaster and I got worked up. A lot. While reading At Peace I felt angry, annoyed, frustrated, extremely sad, yet at the same time I was happy. Happy for Joe, Violet, and her daughte</span>
  <span id="freeText6541454052498359216" style="display:none"><b>“Without peace of mind, life is just a shadow of its possibilities.” <br />- by Jean Borysenko -<br /> <br />3.5 stars.<br /> <br />About my rating: Despite my issues it’s a well-written, emotional and engrossing story and therefore I rounded up to 4 stars.</b><br /><br />Wow, deep breath...I know, I know, hold your horses, Baba! This was such an emotional rollercoaster and I got worked up. A lot. While reading At Peace I felt angry, annoyed, frustrated, extremely sad, yet at the same time I was happy. Happy for Joe, Violet, and her daughters.<br /><br /><i>Brief synopsis</i><br />Violet Winters is a widow with two teenage daughters. During a cold winter night she has to leave her house to tell her annoying neighbor to turn the music down. That's when she meets Joe (Cal) Callahan - her hot-as-shit, bad boy, player, security expert neighbor. Violet's husband was executed by her stalker and even now he is obsessed and can't let her go. Cal's grandfather's sister married a Giglia and the Giglia's are big time mob. They fight against Hart (Violet's stalker). Cal had briefly worked security for Giglia during the last war Giglia had with Hart. And Cal lost his cousin to that war. For that reason Joe has a personal interest to protect Violet and her girls against Hart.<br /><br /><i>What did work for me</i><br />As always Kristen writes terrific family dynamics, good dialogs, and wonderfully fleshed out main and secondary characters. Her writing is not polished, yet it is always honest, real, and emotional. What she writes is really heartfelt, and it is just not essential to write down a “perfect” story. <br /><br />At the beginning of the plot Joe seemed a little bit over the top alpha for my liking. I don’t know, it was just…too much! He was really harsh and rude. Sweet Dream’s Tate Jackson was a badass alpha male but if you compare these two…wow, I’d say Tate is a pussycat compared to Joe. Well, I have to take up the cudgels for Joe, though. As the story unfolds The Lone Wolf became more accessible and kind of more soft. It was a nice change! Moreover, Joe came to love Violet’s girls. It was so sweet to see him interact with these two teenagers. He cared deeply for them and he wanted to protect them. <br /><br />The passion, the hunger, the need between Joe and Vi was palpable. Their chemistry was very good, although there were many ambivalent feelings between these two as well. As always a better communication would have resolved many problems, then again it suited the taciturn and closed off hero. <br /><br />Basically, I liked Violet. I appreciated the fact that she is a very determined and independent single mother. Vi loves her girls deeply and she is there for them and gives her best. She deals with her problems and she does it on her own. With that said, I had my issues and was disappointed when she was “fooling” around with Mike (see spoiler below).<br />Vi really liked Mike but ultimately she chose Joe because she needed him to breathe. Joe bears his own hell and Vi made him feel <b>AT PEACE</b> again. Overall I think they fit perfectly.<br /><br />One of the best aspects of At Peace was the part where a very dear person died. Wow, this was so utterly intense and very, very hard to take. Honestly, I was bawling my eyes out because their pain was my pain. The whole process of getting to know that he died and then accepting the anger, the pain, the solace and ultimately attending the funeral was incredibly well written. Absolutely outstanding!<br /> <br /> <br /> <br /><i>What didn’t work for me</i><br /> <br /><b>**********CONTAINS SPOILERS*******</b><br /> <br />At the beginning Joe annoyed me and acted like a jerk at times. Further, Joe was way too taciturn. He should have talked to Violet earlier. And Joe…you should have come clean. Ever heard of how to avoid heartache??? He posed with an ex in front of his house and of course in front of Violet and her girls to push her away. Joe wanted to save Violet from him. But he didn’t have the balls to end their relationship and that’s why he thought she would do it for him when she “caught” him kissing his ex. And she did. He even confirmed that he did have sex with his ex to push Vi over the ledge (of course he didn't have sex with his ex). It wasn’t only Joe’s fault though. After starting her affair with Joe, Violet went out to Feb's bar and met Mike. She started to flirt with Mike and that's where it all started No qualms at all. Both of them were no saints and they made mistakes. Sometimes Vi was just bitching around which was not funny either. Then again, real life is neither polished nor perfect. <br /> <br />Mr. Jerk was having a meaningful conversation with Ms. Bitch. He’s staking his claim “You’re mine, the girls are mine. I’m stakin’ my claim with you right now and, you force it, I’ll do it with him too.” Oh, Joe, I agree – do it! Holy crap, I was thinking “Please spare me such agonizing pain in the future”, and to top it off what does Ms. Bitch? Why, yes, the same f***ing day she’s hopping to Mike’s townhouse and ends up in his bed. I mean Joe is telling her that she is the only woman on his mind and he didn’t have sex with his ex and what does Vi, what does she?? I was fuming, believe me! Oh, and read that…Vi and Mike are lying in his bed and she says that Mike is winning her over for one night, and that’s why I thought they did the deed. Jeeeez, I get worked up all over again! Will I ever live this down? Holy hell, get this, she says she didn’t have sex with Mike, since they were giving head to each other. WTF…hello???? Uhm, a bit too contradictory for my liking.<br />A few times I caught myself thinking “Woman make up your mind already!” and Joe…tsk-tsk…speak up and get your act together, man!!!<br /> <br />Another weird thing. Frankly, I had to put up with Ty calling his woman “mama” in Lady Luck, which BTW was really sweet and endearing after I got used to it. It kind of fit. However Joe calling Violet “buddy” (besides “baby” and “babe”) felt kind of odd. Gosh, I had to scratch my head. Seriously, if my boyfriend would call me buddy I’d have to inflict some bodily harm.<br /><br /><br />Memorable "quotes"/lines: (SPOILERS)<br /><br />&lt;…&gt;Before she opened it, she turned back. "You don't know, Cal, you have no idea. You've shut yourself up for so long in this fucking house with your tragic memories, you have no idea what's about to walk out your door. Kate, Keira and me, we could have plugged that hole. We could have filled you so full, you'd be bursting. We would have loved that chance. We'd have given it everything we had, no matter the time that slid by, graduations, weddings, grand babies, you'd have been a part of us and we'd have given everything we had to keep you so full, you'd be bursting."&lt;…&gt;<br /><br />&lt;…&gt;It hit him the minute he saw Vi standing, shoeless, carrying a dust rag, wearing shorts and a tank the first time he'd seen her in two and a half months and she was shrieking, fuck, the sound of her shrieking the word "no". He'd never forget it, not in his life. That word, the way she said it, seared a path straight through him.<br />And it kept coming when he ran to her house after the crashing sounds came from it, the Dad pounding on the door.<br />And more of it came when he forced his way in and he saw her, that loss claiming her expression, fresh this time, so difficult to witness he felt it settling on his fucking soul.<br />And more of it came when she pressed into him, giving him her grief.<br />And more, when Kate beat at him, and more when she collapsed into him under the weight of her sorrow.<br />And more when they all curled into him, one by one.<br />And now, that feeling in the left side of his chest wasn't nagging.<br />It was constant, but it wasn't pain.<br />He felt full.<br />Christ, the way it felt, he was full to bursting.&lt;…&gt;<br /><br />&lt;…&gt;"You're mine, the girls are mine. I'm stakin' my claim with you right now and, you force it, I'll do it with him too."&lt;…&gt;<br /><br />&lt;…&gt;"Yeah, you lose this attitude, I can help you work that hurt out."<br />Who was this man? He held onto his tragedy for seventeen fucking years, how could he stand there and tell me he could help me work through mine? &lt;…&gt; "You're unbelievable," I snapped.<br />"I'm yours."<br />That socked me in the gut too, so hard it winded me and all I could do was stare up at him.&lt;…&gt; "You're under my skin."<br />"Please -"<br />"Im under yours."&lt;…&gt;<br /><br />&lt;…&gt;"Gotta remind you," he murmured.<br />We locked eyes.<br />Then he moved.<br />I turned and ran.&lt;…&gt;He was wrong. I remembered. I remembered every second with him, even the ones when we weren't having sex, and I missed them. God, so much, I had to bury it, covering it with everything I had so it wouldn't break me.<br />But it all came back, the longing, the hurt, the hunger, everything we were, everything I wanted us to be and it was everything there was.<br />We tore at each other's clothes, yanking them off while we wrestled for supremacy, kissing, licking, biting, touching, scratching. "Christ, baby," Joe growled…&lt;…&gt;<br /><br />&lt;…&gt;"It was a shit time for you, the worst, but you were there and you saw 'em doin' it. They crawled into this same fuckin' bed with me, so did you, and when you did, you all became mine."<br />"That's insane," I informed him.<br />"That's the way it is," he shot back.<br />"Joe, we were beside ourselves with grief."<br />"Yeah, and when you are you don't lock tight to some guy you don't know or some asshole you hate. You lock tight to what's yours to remind yourself that it is and that you need it."<br />"That wasn't what was happening."<br />"Buddy, you're naked in my lap, your girls want me in the house, you're pissed at me, tellin' yourself it's over and all I gotta do is kiss you and you turn wild. This shit gonna sink in?"<br />"It did twice," I reminded him, "and no matter the signals you gave me, Joe, it wasn't what I thought."<br />"Not given' you signals this time, Vi, I'm telling' you straight out and I'll tell you somethin' else, always listen to your gut."<br />"Joe -"<br />"It told you you belonged to me, I'm tellin' you it was right."&lt;…&gt;<br /><br />&lt;…&gt;"He promised me, I stand down, he'd give you everything."<br />My heart flipped over.<br />"He did?"<br />"Yeah," Mike nodded, then his hands tightened on my jaws. "He doesn't, Vi, you come to me and I'll give it to you."&lt;…&gt;"Sweetheart," Mike called and I opened my eyes. "You won't be comin' to me. Man I talked to today would move heaven and earth to give everything to you."<br />"Mike -"<br />"Didn't think that, no fuckin' way I'd stand down."<br />"Mike -"<br />His lips touched mine again and when his head lifted, he whispered, "Be happy, honey."<br />I nodded and whispered back, "You too, Mike."<br />He smiled and it was the first time he smiled at me in the hundreds he'd given me that it didn't reach his eyes.&lt;…&gt;<br /><br />&lt;…&gt;She ended with her knees to the floor, her body between his legs, her torso in Joe's lap, her face in his chest, her arms wrapped around him and, before I could open my mouth or even more, she burst into tears.<br />"I knew you were always lookin' out for us," she cried into his chest, "I knew it!"<br />That lump hit my throat again but it was so big this time, it choked me.<br />Joe's hand dropped to Keira's hair and he bent forward. "Baby, hey," he whispered.<br />"I knew it!" she sobbed into his stomach.<br />What I knew was this wasn't about Joe and the dog. This was about my sweet, crazy, strong, beautiful daughter losing her Dad and losing her XXXXX and living in a world that was uncertain, being afraid of that world and needing something to hold onto. They'd been strong a long time, both my girls had. And I was proud of them. But even the strongest person in the world needed something to hold onto.&lt;…&gt;"Keirry, honey, what's this?" Joe whispered into her ear when he had her in his arms and she'd burrowed in closer. He, too, knew it wasn't about the dog.<br />She yanked her head out of his neck, looked at him and demanded in a fierce tone, "Don't ever go away, Joe."<br />At my daughter's words, I felt my breath choke me so hard I heard it too and that choking sound wasn't just coming from me.<br />"I'm not goin' anywhere, honey," Joe replied gently.<br />"Promise!"&lt;…&gt;"I promise," Joe said, his tone just as fierce, then he put an arm behind her knees and he straightened from the chair, Keira held to his chest.<br />I straightened too, murmuring, "Joe."<br />"I got this, buddy."<br />"Joe -"<br />"Got it," Joe repeated and walked from the room down the hall.<br />I stood there, staring down the hall. Then I turned and stared at our group, seeing Bea and Theresa flat out crying.&lt;…&gt;<br /><br />&lt;…&gt;He's here, buddy, that's all I could take, that's all I need. I had to let go the rest. The rest is too much," he told me.<br />I was a mother and I was a widow. I knew better than that.<br />"You need all you can get," I whispered.<br />"Can't take anymore," he replied.<br />I pressed my hand into his chest. "That just isn't true."<br />"Vi -"<br />"Bring him home."<br />"Violet -"<br />"Let me bring him home."<br />"Buddy -"<br />I pulled my hand from his and put it back to his face. "He's a part of you and I want you, all of you. I want my girls to have all of you. Joe, honey, please let me bring him home."<br />We stared at each other again for a long time before Joe whispered a tortured, "Fuck…get it." &lt;…&gt; "You looked AT PEACE." My tears could be heard in my words but Joe's eyes didn't move from the picture.<br />"I had the world sleepin' on my chest," he replied, his voice low, thick.<br />I looked at the photo. "Funny how the world can fit in your arm."&lt;…&gt;<br /><br /><br /><b>************END OF SPOILERS***********</b><br /><br /><br />BTW, the suspense part of At Peace was absolutely minor. Overall it was a very engaging and certainly worthwhile story. If you can bear the “flaws” I mentioned, then I would recommend you to read At Peace.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6541454052498359216" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a href="http://www.google.com/imgres?hl=en&amp;gbv=2&amp;biw=1080&amp;bih=520&amp;tbs=itp:face&amp;tbm=isch&amp;tbnid=CQBzGjrYHy1e7M:&amp;imgrefurl=http://newsregale39spite.blog.fc2.com/blog-entry-26.html&amp;docid=qLZFw4wG9LqUyM&amp;imgurl=http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_cGNRz9dYB4w/TEgnPEWbvwI/AAAAAAAACz4/zGyizuWu2lo/s1600/Claudia_Maio2010_GiseleBundchen_phPatrickDemarchelier_02.jpg&amp;w=500&amp;h=686&amp;ei=-nQgT9X_IsbiiAKRsMHICw&amp;zoom=1&amp;iact=hc&amp;vpx=226&amp;vpy=124&amp;dur=2772&amp;hovh=263&amp;hovw=192&amp;tx=106&amp;ty=187&amp;sig=107001603571935061623&amp;page=5&amp;tbnh=156&amp;tbnw=119&amp;start=73&amp;ndsp=21&amp;ved=1t:429,r:1,s:73" rel="nofollow noopener"></a>

</div><br><br><br><b>
  <u>My Kate &amp; Keira</u>
</b><br><br><div>
  <a href="http://pinterest.com/pin/489133209499058399/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416260268i/11924070._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="295" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><div>
  <p>
    <a href="http://idthrowglitterintheair.tumblr.com/post/32438220064" rel="nofollow noopener"></a>
    <a href="http://pinterest.com/vikafika/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"></a>
    <a href="http://pinterest.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"></a>
  </p>
</div><br><br>Vi and her 2 teenage daughters, Kate &amp; Keira, are newcomers to the 'Burg. Escaping a psychopathic criminal stalker who killed her cop husband. Violet is a great mom doing everything a great mom does who doesn't have her partner... gently spoiling her daughters because of that. Vi living for her daughters in grief for over a year.<br><br>Joe is a security to the stars, who barely visit his home... a home that is right next door to Vi. Joe lives smart taking jobs that will take him that much faster to cushy retirements BUT at the same time he is not living. He is a man that lives in his grief for 17 years.<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/560/tumblrlg44rqrzuw1qgjm3a.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380381404ra/738707.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"He needs Mom and us more than we need him. He needs a family. He's over there, all by himself, he has nobody. We have each other. He needs somebody. I can tell."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>... and Joe did not stand a chance living next door to that Trio. From Vi's midnight visit, Katy's too-mature wariness of Joe yet lassoing him in into the fold and Keiry's open-hearted-arm-flailing acceptance that is just pure heart melting. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Like their mother, they were sucking him in, using him to plug that hole their father left and their combined power was almost unbeatable.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Oooh Joe tries to keep them at arm's length... VERY HARD... pulling all the stops making him the jerkiest of all Jerks in KA Kingdom. However, he is also the hottest. Joe is just as confused in his protectiveness and papa-bear behavior of the girls as Vi is clueless in how she lassos in men in and being all organically flirty. But disaster after disaster with Vi's stalker destroying her in an effort to "catch" her attention Joe can't/doesn't have it in him to stay away. THANK. FUCKING. GOD! Just 'cause they didn't start out 'that way'... it ended up being so. much. more.<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/22/tumblrmje6dm5uyk1s2z8g7.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380381404ra/738708.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>There are some awesome characters who are introduced and some old ones that make a special appearance. Holla to Mama Jackie! That woman is amazing.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Feb lost the man who helped her breath, didn't take a full breath for twenty years until she got him back... You lost your man, your brother and honey, my heart's with you, that's awful... You two come with so much baggage, it's a wonder you don't' get crushed. And that's the thing, neither of you did. And you found each other. It's time to unload that burden and fine some joy."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Feb, Colt and baby Jack... so happy for them! <br><br>Mikey... um... sorry man. Your turn comes in book #4. You are a nice man but you are not Vi's. <br><br>Now my favorites: Benny &amp; Frankie - WHEN ARE WE FINALLY GETTING THEIR STORY??? I've read this series over a year ago... re-reading now and STILL the story is not out.<br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/534/tumblrm8vw4jy1wv1rqpx0x.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380381404ra/738709.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/855/oie201540mrjnjmjp.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380381404i/738710.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><b>If you haven't realized it yet it is my favorite book of the series... no it's in the top 3 of my favorite KA writings.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="3541885933981715308" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText12932809560359553409" style="display:none">Still one of my favorite KA books!<br />LOVE VI-0H-MY and Joe (Cal) Callihan. &lt;3<br /><br />Third read: 'cause I'm in the mood for a KA romancin', a little Vi-oh-my (Violet), and a whole lotta Mr Joe Callihan (security to the stars).<br /><br />Second Read: July 13, 2014<br /><br />LOVE! <br /><br />First Read: March 30, 2012<br />5 ++<br /><br />This bloody book had me in knots &amp; stitches the whole time! <div id="review_333361449" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/333361449" />
    <a title="Dija" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2857113-dija"><img alt="Dija" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1360335537p2/2857113.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/333361449?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dija" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dija" href="/user/show/2857113-dija">Dija</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=2011">2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=meh">meh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=cotton-candy-fluff">cotton-candy-fluff</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=could-have-been-sooo-much-better">could-have-been-sooo-much-better</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=cr">cr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=everyone-loved-but-dija">everyone-loved-but-dija</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=authors-i-stalk">authors-i-stalk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=great-disappointment">great-disappointment</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=my-reviews">my-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer333361449" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9557468937203905406"><b>Rating:</b> A very, very generous two stars.<br/><br/>Before I begin my rant (because that's pretty much all this review is), I'd like to clarify something: I <i>adore</i> Kristen Ashley. To me, she's the Walt Disney of adult fiction. Her stories are unforgettable, fulfilling, and utterly beautiful. <br/><br/>That being said, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11665750.At_Peace__The__Burg___2_' title='At Peace (The 'Burg, #2) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>At Peace</a> didn't do it for me. <i>At all</i>. I had a number of issues with this book, and most of them are because of the heroine, Violet.<br/><br/>To begin with, the relationship between Violet and Tim, her first husban</span>
  <span id="freeText9557468937203905406" style="display:none"><b>Rating:</b> A very, very generous two stars.<br /><br />Before I begin my rant (because that's pretty much all this review is), I'd like to clarify something: I <i>adore</i> Kristen Ashley. To me, she's the Walt Disney of adult fiction. Her stories are unforgettable, fulfilling, and utterly beautiful. <br /><br />That being said, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11665750.At_Peace__The__Burg___2_" title="At Peace (The 'Burg, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">At Peace</a> didn't do it for me. <i>At all</i>. I had a number of issues with this book, and most of them are because of the heroine, Violet.<br /><br />To begin with, the relationship between Violet and Tim, her first husband, wasn't really explained that well. They were together for nearly two decades but right after she jumped into bed with another man, she barely thought about him. That's not only weird, but highly unrealistic as well. <br /><br />And throughout the story, she never felt guilty about sleeping with or loving someone else. I understand about moving on, but some people you just never fully get over (especially not a little over two years later), and one of them should be your husband of 20 years. So either her relationship with Tim wasn't as perfect as is portrayed or she really didn't love him as much as she supposedly claimed. Either way, I would have appreciated the story a lot more if there had been further clarification about where exactly Violet and Tim stood as a couple.<br /><br />Onto the present romance. To sum it up, I couldn't <i>believe</i> how Violet acted. The fuck, calling cheating and leading a poor man on as "looking out for myself" while sleeping regularly with another man, and when the former confronts you about it, having a breakdown and acting like <i>you</i>'ve been the one wronged in all of this?! Uggghhh!! This woman got on my very last nerve, I swear.<br /><br />Another constant wtf moment? Whenever anyone went on and on and freakin' <i>on</i> about what a "prize" Violet was (I know that's a KA constant, but it really bugged me in this one). I tried hard to be forgiving and all, but a two-timing cow is a two-timing cow and that sorta wipes out a lot of the good, yes? It does as far as I'm concerned.<br /><br />I only began to stop hating her after 81% (yes, I was keeping track). And I only fully stopped hating her at 97%.<br /><br />Surprisingly, I didn't hate Joe all that much. I disliked him immensely but I never felt he was being two-faced (unlike a certain someone else, ahem). I eventually came to like him, but I don't think I'll ever <i>love</i> him.<br /><br />The only highlight in this loooong book was the budding romance between Benny and Frankie. I'm absolutely ecstatic they'll be getting their own book soon. My initial plan after finishing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11665750.At_Peace__The__Burg___2_" title="At Peace (The 'Burg, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">At Peace</a> was to give up on the rest of the series, but I'll be reading on because I'm highly interested in reading Mike and Benny's respective books. <i>Really</i> hope they're both better than this one.<br /><br /><b>For more reviews, visit my <a href="http://zombiehazard.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a>.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9557468937203905406" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_329833389" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/329833389" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/329833389?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=suspenseful">suspenseful</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer329833389" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4878504425716184824"><b>*3.5 Stars*</b><br/><br/>Another sensuous, action-packed installment to The 'Burg series. <i>At Peace</i> was a fun, exciting read filled with tension, romance, suspense, and one agonizingly sexy alpha-hero. <br/><br/><b>Cal</b> and <b>Violet</b> are neighbors whose friendship takes a little longer to ignite than their passion. The sexy, brooding, tormented Cal has been burned in a past relationship and is emotionally distant and unattainable. Violet has moved into the neighborhood with her two daughters to escape the threat of her husband</span>
  <span id="freeText4878504425716184824" style="display:none"><b>*3.5 Stars*</b><br><br>Another sensuous, action-packed installment to The 'Burg series. <i>At Peace</i> was a fun, exciting read filled with tension, romance, suspense, and one agonizingly sexy alpha-hero. <br><br><b>Cal</b> and <b>Violet</b> are neighbors whose friendship takes a little longer to ignite than their passion. The sexy, brooding, tormented Cal has been burned in a past relationship and is emotionally distant and unattainable. Violet has moved into the neighborhood with her two daughters to escape the threat of her husband's killer, who happens to be stalking her. Cal, being in the line of security, decides to protect Violet and her daughters when they learn that the stalker has found their new location. This begins the turbulent but extremely sexy-sweet journey of Cal and Vi.<br><br>The characters in this story are so realistically portrayed and hold a familiar connection to one another, however, I was hoping for a bit more distinction between each personality; all too often, I found the characters blending into one. I really adored watching the relationship between Cal and Violet's daughters blossom. I loved that the emotional connection between Cal and Vi grew slowly and eventually caught up with their initial attraction. I think anyone who has read a KA book pretty much knows what to expect regarding the racy, no holds barred steam factor, and this book certainly makes no exception.<br><br>While I can appreciate the great attention to detail Kristen Ashley displays in her writing, I feel its intricacies immensly drag out the story. I also find myself getting a little tripped up on some of the awkwardly structured sentences which took away from an otherwise intriguing plot. That being said, KA does have such a distinctive, recognizable writing style and I can see why there are so many Kristen Ashley addicts out there. Fun read! <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Maximum steam<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Slow burn. Intense and sexy. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Alpha, protective hero. Sweet but strong heroine.<br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> A steamy, suspenseful love story with a great portrayal of friendship and family. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Highly descriptive. Slightly repetitive. Engaging.<br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person Perspective: Heroine<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Character spinoff<br><b>▪ HEA? </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer251874834" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13890887996971394080"><b>5+ stars</b><br/><br/>I think I love Joe (Cal) Callahan, security specialist, as much or at least close to my feelings for Tate from Sweet Dreams!<br/> <br/>Why?!?! I’m not sure! Except I do have a weakness for those totally over the top badass hotties. Yeah, like Tate, Hawk, and Ty, Joe fits right in with them. He’s gruff, blunt, callous and can be downright vicious! He appears heartless AND he is a player! He doesn’t do “relationships” and can be very brutal to get this point across. “We’re done” is one way of statin</span>
  <span id="freeText13890887996971394080" style="display:none"><b>5+ stars</b><br /><br />I think I love Joe (Cal) Callahan, security specialist, as much or at least close to my feelings for Tate from Sweet Dreams!<br /> <br />Why?!?! I’m not sure! Except I do have a weakness for those totally over the top badass hotties. Yeah, like Tate, Hawk, and Ty, Joe fits right in with them. He’s gruff, blunt, callous and can be downright vicious! He appears heartless AND he is a player! He doesn’t do “relationships” and can be very brutal to get this point across. “We’re done” is one way of stating it’s over! He would not win “best sweet romantic hero of the year” but all the ladies in this Burg sure stop and gawk when he is near.<br /> <br />Along with his harsh behavior, he’s also a smart, protective, gorgeous, sexy as sin, tall and a rippled muscled body hunk. I think Violet says it well, <i> “his body is far more beautiful out of clothes than in them.”</i> Whew! <br /> <br />At the very beginning he hurts Violet to the core and then does it again! And I do like Violet Winters. Not only did I like her, I admired her. There were times I didn’t like her choices and I wanted to shake her! It took a long while for me to understand where she was coming from and what caused her to make these choices. And to top it all off, something happens in this book that I usually can not tolerate in my romances! And yet, I can easily say this is one of the best KA’s I’ve read. I loved it! It was intense, emotional, and I could hardly put it down. I hated for this book to end!<br /><br />Violet has spent eighteen years married to her high school sweetheart. He filled her life with joy and they have two wonderful teenage daughters. He was a dedicated police officer in Chicago until one day a madman became obsessed with his wife and put a bullet in his head. Now, nearly two years later, Vi has taken her daughters and fled Chicago hoping to escape this crazed stalker. She is now Joe’s neighbor and immediately upon meeting him, there is chemistry! <br /><br /><i> “It was wild, almost a struggle. I couldn’t get enough of him, take enough from him. No matter what I got, I wanted more, like a craving that hollowed out my insides, needing to be filled.” </i><br /><br />I think KA did a great job as we watch Joe and Violet both evolve into amazing! I came to understand why Joe avoids relationships as his dark secrets are revealed. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I also understand why Vi would feel more comfortable being with someone who was more like her dead husband, Tim. After all, he is the only man she’s ever been with romantically and sexually until Joe. Finally getting this did help calm my frustrations with her. I still didn't like what happened, but I understood it better.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />It was great catching up with Colt and Feb who are also neighbors. And as with KAs other books, the secondary characters are a delightful lot especially Vi’s two teenage daughters along with Joe’s extended Italian family. The family pull here is tender and very real. The interaction and closeness that develops between Joe and Violet’s girls is heartwarming. They needed him and he needs them. And be forewarned, there is a heartbreaking scene that will have you in tears! Deeply touching, deeply sad!<br /><br />For me, this was another great read from Kristen Ashley! In this second installment we meet many new characters. I’m hoping that Bennie and Frankie will get their own book along with Detective Mike Haines.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13890887996971394080" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer268030289" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6680744838964139284">5 stars – Contemporary Romance/Romantic Suspense<br/><br/>Wow! I <i>loved</i> this! Kristen Ashley is an amazing author warrior queen! Seriously! <b>
  <i>At Peace</i>
</b> is the 8th book of hers that I’ve read and highly enjoyed and it’s one of my favorite KA reads. Although the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series and my beloved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_' title='Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Law Man</a> still hold a definite edge.<br/><br/>Joe Callahan is another extremely domineering, uber alpha asshat and lordy have mercy did he piss me off...until around the 80% mark that is! There were times I swore that ev</span>
  <span id="freeText6680744838964139284" style="display:none">5 stars – Contemporary Romance/Romantic Suspense<br><br>Wow! I <i>loved</i> this! Kristen Ashley is an amazing author warrior queen! Seriously! <b>
  <i>At Peace</i>
</b> is the 8th book of hers that I’ve read and highly enjoyed and it’s one of my favorite KA reads. Although the <i>Colorado Mountain</i> series and my beloved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_" title="Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Law Man</a> still hold a definite edge.<br><br>Joe Callahan is another extremely domineering, uber alpha asshat and lordy have mercy did he piss me off...until around the 80% mark that is! There were times I swore that even if he got down on his hands and knees and crawled through broken glass to apologize, plead, and beg for forgiveness for being such an absolute d*ck that I wouldn’t have been swayed. I mean, I wanted him to execute some serious groveling. Alas, he never did. BUT, his way of making amends was much more subtle, genuine, powerful, and affecting and therefore all the more gratifying. And in the end, he totally won me over and had me sighing and swooning along with the Winters girls.<br><br>So Joe was an arrogant jerk and Violet could be a wishy-washy wimp at times, but boy were they explosive together! The sex scenes were rough and smokin’ <i>hot</i>! And I was anxious for them to find their HEA. The love triangle between Joe/Violet/Mike lasted far too long, and I missed Ashley’s staple, celebrated, detailed epilogue, but otherwise this is another fabulous KA winner! <br><br>I’m looking forward to reading Mike’s story, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13497180.Games_of_the_Heart__The__Burg___4_" title="Games of the Heart (The 'Burg, #4) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Games of the Heart</a>, because he’s certainly due a much deserved HEA. And I read on the author’s website that she’s planning to write Frankie and Benny’s story in an upcoming <i>‘Burg</i> release. Yay! Kristen Ashley has already solidified a position as one of my top favorite keeper authors of 2012. Big 5 stars!<br><br>I had a hard time finding my perfect Joe because he’s so enigmatically, broodingly sexy and all badass, rugged alpha male with some macho Italian mixed in, but I think Italian actor Raoul Bova could fit the bill.<br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=3282366_gal.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380368328i/720885._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=imagesqtbnANd9GcSUy4hZZbwOWenOM3lC723oEVUuZVZFq6Muf2GCjOa6m3LhZP6iPXrXTVbr.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380368328i/720886.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=11238730_gal.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380368328i/720887.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>

<div id="review_2092641422" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2092641422" />
    <a title="~Mindy Lynn~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7320000-mindy-lynn"><img alt="~Mindy Lynn~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604190846p2/7320000.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2092641422?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~Mindy Lynn~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~Mindy Lynn~" href="/user/show/7320000-mindy-lynn">~Mindy Lynn~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=alpha-s-bb">alpha-s-bb</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=damaged-and-broken">damaged-and-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=2017-challenge">2017-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=assholes-we-love">assholes-we-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=show-me-the-money">show-me-the-money</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=girls-who-love-boys">girls-who-love-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=bad-boy-love">bad-boy-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7320000-mindy-lynn?shelf=freebies">freebies</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2092641422" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7210570141295275508">Gawd, I forgot how long this book was. Still love it though!<br/><br/>It's a bit surprising how much I have grown as a reader since reading this book the first time. I found the second time around with this book that I was picking at the female more. It surprised me because I really liked her the first time around and I still liked her, I just found things about her that annoyed me and some other things in the book that annoyed me as a whole. But not enough to un-claim this one as my favorite in the serie</span>
  <span id="freeText7210570141295275508" style="display:none">Gawd, I forgot how long this book was. Still love it though!<br /><br />It's a bit surprising how much I have grown as a reader since reading this book the first time. I found the second time around with this book that I was picking at the female more. It surprised me because I really liked her the first time around and I still liked her, I just found things about her that annoyed me and some other things in the book that annoyed me as a whole. But not enough to un-claim this one as my favorite in the series. I think I have all around grown more critical of the M/F books I read. But it's KA and I know what I am getting when I crack one of her books open. I <b>know</b> that the females are going to roll over and do what their men want them to do. I <b>know</b> that the female will put up a good bitch fest until the guy says something sweet that makes her go all dick-dumb. I <b>know</b> that the men use sex a lot to shut their women up when they feel they're right and the woman just needs to accept it with some dick to go with it. <b>THIS</b> is <b>KA</b>. I've loved her since her Rock Chick books and will continue to love her. I haven't loved all her books. I have even really disliked a couple. But a couple dislikes won't turn me off from reading her books just like the way she writes her females a bit on the weak side won't keep me from reading her books. It's not her fault that I can't relate to these females when they go belly up. I am not made that way. But I do usually like her characters and her plot lines. And even though I would probably never end a fight with a guy even if he was right because I am that damn proud, I love me some of these Alpha males that she writes about. I'd never give in, but I'd be all over them for some sexy times. So maybe I should take it easy on some of these females. LOL<br /><br />I said this book is long, and baby it is. But I got so sucked in to it (yes, even the 2nd time reading it) that I didn't feel the length. I did feel the damn migraine I got when I finished it because of all the damn crying I did. Dolls, I am not a very emotional gal, but damn if this book didn't have my younger sister howling with laughter at me when she caught me crying over this damn story more than a few times. YES, I said MORE than a few times. Its just got some horribly sad stuff in it and I was obviously feeling very emotional about it all. It hit all the feels my peeps. <br />Joe/Cal is what draws me in with this story. I love him. He's a complete asshole, but you all know we all love us some asshole men. We love catching them and getting their sweet. But I also enjoyed all the side characters and how they all played a specific role that moved the story along. <br /><br />I think I might visit more books from this series in the coming weeks/months. <br /><br />Happy reading dolls! xx<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7210570141295275508" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YD/ly6/nZGq9TiqUuw1Soqh0rWA5C9S61GLavZcwLY3wu9YC1Kc4g5g+fWHftj3T8v8zSpFtaMTLszNIDq0mEg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZFJx8+1p72g/s48xGsJsEkT+LWGstQgHwjtivPmNkQL01kI6limzgRrD2MR+eQNjHnWzSwTTtHnd6otJYBCanQ==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText9291526585456891269" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>

We’d have given it everything we had, no matter the time that slid by, graduations, weddings, grandbabies, you’d have been a part of us and we’d have given everything we had to keep you<br />so full, you’d be bursting.”<br />Cal didn’t reply.<br />“Joe,” she whispered, “you let me walk out this door, you’ll lose your chance.”<br />Cal didn’t move.<br />Vi waited.<br />Cal stayed seated.&rdquo;</span>
